Current Commentary

The Completion of the Cemetery for Fallen Soldiers 38

— Du

Yesterday, the capital city held the completion ceremony and service for the Cemetery for Fallen Soldiers of the National Revolutionary Army. From Chairman Lin and Chairman Chiang to the ministers and high-ranking officials, all attended the memorial service. All members of the Central Committee and representatives from the Fifth National Congress also went to participate. The occasion was grand and fervent, with the entire city eager to witness the model of the martyrs and inspire the reverie of future generations. Its significance is considerable.

The Cemetery for Fallen Soldiers was built with funds allocated by the Central Party Headquarters. Preparations began in 1929, and construction officially started in the spring of 1931. In addition to the cemetery, there are ancillary buildings such as a memorial hall, a memorial tower, and decorative archways. The exterior is extremely magnificent, and the layout is solemn and orderly. Furthermore, its location to the east of the Premier's mausoleum is sufficient to demonstrate unwavering loyalty, enduring beyond life and death. The heroic souls within all returned from campaigns and battles, directly or indirectly under the leadership of the Premier, to express their sincere devotion. Now that the National Revolutionary Army has celebrated its success, the blood and bodies of these people have long since mingled with the yellow earth and disappeared. The martyrs sacrificed themselves for righteousness, not counting their own posthumous recognition. However, the authorities, mindful of their comrades-in-arms, did not want to be alone in enjoying their honor. Therefore, they wanted to create a concrete memorial to mark their eternal memory, which is a rational and necessary step.

Furthermore, we have something more to say. The psychology of most citizens is accustomed to weakness and reluctant to be vigorous, and this has not been the case for just a day or two. The way to correct and encourage this lies in using the spirit of the martyrs as a model for the world to emulate. In a time of national darkness and ignorance, the National Revolutionary Army engaged in the work of destruction and purification. The martyrs fought bravely, risking their lives and regarding death as returning home. Their impassioned and heroic spirit can serve as a standard for the time. Although the times have changed today, the existence of this magnificent cemetery in the capital, a place where diverse people gather, will not fail to inspire admiration and longing. Moreover, the interior and exterior of the memorial tower are still filled with stirring words such as the Premier's opening speech and farewell speech at the Whampoa Military Academy. Those who set foot inside can gain inspiration through browsing. Its benefit to people's hearts is not insignificant. From this perspective, the construction of the Cemetery for Fallen Soldiers will not only strengthen the weak and establish courage, inspiring future generations, but also provide solace to the heroic souls and ensure their immortality.

Abyssinian Troops Complete Deployment; Major Battle Imminent on the Northern Front 39

Large detachments encircle Italian troops on the flanks; counterattack begins on the southern front at dawn.

Addis Ababa: The Abyssinian army's preparations to defend against enemy troops are almost complete. The Emperor has left the capital by plane today. From the current situation, the first major engagement is now taking place in the vicinity of Magaal on the northern front. A column of Abyssinian troops is now advancing towards Sereka, about 100 miles south of Magaal. The number of Abyssinian troops assembled in that area is estimated to be between 15,000 and 20,000. The Emperor's hunting chief, Ayal, has launched a vigorous counterattack in the south, between Annal (which the Abyssinian army claims to have recovered on November 16) and Golahei. The battle began at dawn today, and it is reported that the enemy troops have suffered heavy losses. By noon, the Abyssinian army claimed to have recovered the Italian positions. The Abyssinian army is now planning to attack the left flank of the Italian troops near Annal. Lieutenant Colonel Julian, known as the "Harlem Black Eagle," recently resigned from his position in the Emperor's service. Today, he told a Reuters reporter that if the Abyssinian army does not change its strategy, Abyssinia is in danger of being annexed by Italy. The Abyssinian army only has knives and guns, and its commander wants to follow the Emperor's strategy of concentrated attacks, which makes him particularly disheartened. He trained infantrymen to be proficient in new-style crawling guerrilla tactics, and therefore requested guns and ammunition. The Emperor is of good character, and he wishes to serve him wholeheartedly. Since taking office, he has not received a salary. The Emperor ordered his military officials to issue military equipment, but they were negligent and failed to issue it for a long time, so he resigned. The lieutenant colonel also said that he is very concerned about the Abyssinian army, because they are not suitable for tactics that require the use of tanks, airplanes, and machine guns. If they advance in a concentrated manner, they may be annihilated by the Italian army. When the lieutenant colonel met with the Reuters reporter, he had removed his usual resplendent uniform and was only wearing a short shirt and trousers, with a monocle on the bridge of his nose. After leaving the Emperor, the American black in the service of Abyssinia is now only Mr. Roberson from Chicago. (Reuters dispatch on the 19th)

Italian Front on the Northern Front: Italian outposts in the vicinity of Magaal were surrounded by large detachments of Abyssinian troops today, and a bloody battle is imminent. The Abyssinian army is now planning to attack the flanks of the Italian troops from both the east and west in hopes of retaking Magaal. On the other hand, guerrillas are disrupting the Italian army's rear transportation. Although Italian aircraft bombed extensively on Monday, the Abyssinian army is still firmly entrenched in the trenches around Aba Araci and Assangi. Because the main force of the Italian army has been unable to advance towards Lake Assangi today, military operations have effectively come to a standstill again. (National Telegraph dispatch on the 19th)

Current Status of Sanctions 40

French Reply to Italian Protest, Laval Meets with British Ambassador, German Ambassador Visits the British Foreign Office

(Geneva) The League of Nations Assembly’s Sanctions Coordination Committee will likely convene soon to discuss whether to include kerosene, coal, steel, iron, etc., on the list of raw materials embargoed to Italy. League of Nations officials believe President Roosevelt will submit a bill to Congress to prohibit the export of the aforementioned raw materials to belligerent nations, as Secretary of State Hull previously made such a declaration. Furthermore, the U.S. government has already implemented export controls on the items proposed for embargo by the Canadian representative to the Sanctions Committee. Additionally, the Argentine government has notified the League of Nations that it will prohibit the export of kerosene to Italy. Although Argentina's kerosene production is not significant, the League of Nations officials are satisfied that Argentina's initiative will improve the prospects for future negotiations. Furthermore, the League of Nations has received notifications from Mexico, Norway, the Netherlands, and many other countries, all stating that they will implement sanctions against Italy before November 18th. The Turkish government has notified that it will implement strict measures starting November 18th. Venezuela has announced that it has implemented the first and second types of sanctions plans. Colombia has announced that the trade agreement between Italy and Colombia will be terminated on November 18th. The chairman of the Sanctions Committee, the Portuguese representative Vasconcelos, and various experts are planning to gather reports from various governments on November 25th for review. (Havas, 20th)

(Paris) French Prime Minister Laval today presented the Italian Ambassador with France's response to Italy's protest against sanctions. It is reported that the wording of the French response is very subtle and does not change its policy. It stated that after the League of Nations declared Italy an aggressor, Article 16 of the Covenant naturally came into effect. France respects its signature and, in addition to participating in the economic and financial measures predetermined in Geneva, cannot take other actions. However, the French government has not abandoned hope of resolving and terminating the Italian-Abyssinian war and the restrictions Italy is subject to due to international sanctions through friendly means. Although the British response has not been sent, it is reported that its form and substance are the same as the French response. The British response is currently being distributed to the 52 members of the League of Nations Sanctions Coordination Committee for review. (Reuters, 19th)

(Paris) Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Laval received the Italian Ambassador Cerruti today, personally delivering France's reply to the Italian protest. This reply will be published on Friday and does not contain any new elements. It only explains that since the League of Nations Council and the League of Nations Assembly have clearly identified Italy as an aggressor against Abyssinia, the provisions of Article 16 of the League of Nations Covenant should be implemented. France has an obligation to the League of Nations Covenant and must comply with it, but still hopes that the Italian-Abyssinian dispute can be resolved amicably. (Havas, 19th)

(Paris) Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Laval received the British Ambassador to France, Sir Eric Phipps, this morning for consultations. (Havas, 20th)

(London) The German Ambassador to Britain, Herr von Hoesch, recently visited the Foreign Office for consultations. (Havas, 2nd)

Goods Shipped to Italy via Bremen Increase

(London) In recent weeks, the amount of goods shipped from Germany to Italy via Bremen has increased by 50%. Large quantities of lumber, coal, automobiles, and aircraft parts are now being shipped to Italy. Goods shipped from Italy to Germany are mostly fruits and agricultural products. The increase in German exports to Italy is undoubtedly largely due to the implementation of financial and economic sanctions against Italy by League of Nations member states. Germany is not a member of the League of Nations and is therefore not obligated to participate in these sanctions. (Reuters, 20th)

(Geneva) The Argentine government recently notified League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol that it has included kerosene, coal, steel, iron, etc., in the list of raw materials embargoed to Italy. As for the embargo measures on these raw materials, Canada proposed them. The Sanctions Coordination Committee, considering the implementation of this proposal, requires the assistance of some non-member states such as the United States and Germany, so a decision has not yet been made. Now that Argentina has made the decision, it is enough to lead other member states. (Havas, 19th)

(Brussels) On the 14th of this month, the government issued an order prohibiting the export of munitions and war materials to Italy. Recently, a supplementary order was issued, prohibiting the transportation of ores, bauxite, metals, metal mixtures, and their waste materials to Italy. (Havas, 20th)

(London) In order to prevent Italian goods from entering Britain via countries that refuse to participate in sanctions, the government previously decided that goods imported into Britain from those countries must be presented with a certificate of origin. However, after Germany protested, negotiations were held with Germany, which are still in progress. Recently, Britain intends to enter into a general agreement with various producing countries to prohibit the transportation of kerosene to Italy. (Havas, 20th)

(Turin) The lawn of Crown Prince Umberto's Racconigi estate, originally used for recreation, has recently been converted into a cornfield to increase agricultural production and resist sanctions. (Havas, 20th)

(Rome) The Italian government today continued to issue regulations on the management of goods exports. At the same time, a campaign to boycott foreign goods has been launched throughout the country. It is reported that more than 150,000 merchants have sworn to support the boycott. Today, archbishops in various places have issued church notices, urging believers to make efforts and sacrifices to resist sanctions. In theaters across the country, actors are urging the audience to fight against sanctions. The Fascist Grand Council announced that December 18th will be the date of the next meeting. This move is different from usual practice, so it is taken very seriously. It can be seen that Mussolini intends to have closer cooperation with the Grand Council than before. The regulations published by the government today prohibit the export of goods that are indispensable to domestic needs, such as the chemicals needed to manufacture explosives. It also stipulates that Italian goods can be exported as usual to countries that do not adopt sanctions, but must comply with the current clearing agreements. However, for countries that adopt sanctions, Italian goods cannot be exported unless foreign merchants have bank accounts in Italy and pay for the goods in advance. As for woolen, cotton, and silk goods, they must first obtain a license from a special national agency before they can be exported. (Reuters, 19th)

(Rome) Official circles here indicated today that the League of Nations' sanctions front has cracked. It is reported that some foreign ministers have stated several reservations when accepting the Italian protest. Italian official circles believe that they can negotiate the purchase of various goods, so that the Geneva front cannot be maintained, and thus Italy will not be greatly affected by sanctions. In order to consolidate Italy's financial position, the government has today ordered that the government has the exclusive right to purchase any gold coins abroad. (National Telegram, 19th)

(Port Said) It was learned today that between November 13th and 18th, as many as 14 Italian ships passed through the Suez Canal, carrying a total of 2,624 sick and wounded soldiers back to their home country. (National Telegram, 19th)

(Asmara) The outgoing Commander of the Italian Army in the Northern Theater, General De Bono, passed through here today on his way home. De Bono has handed over command to General Santini temporarily, pending the arrival of Marshal Badoglio. (National News Agency, 20th)

US Congressional Legislation - Hull Issues Statement 41

No Protection for Trade with Belligerent Nations

San Pedro, California, USA. The extent to which the new U.S. neutrality legislation will be implemented is a mystery of the current situation. The statement issued by Secretary of State Hull today to the Pacific Coast Maritime Federation can be regarded as the current interpretation of the law. The Maritime Federation had resolved yesterday to refuse to sail ships carrying military supplies to war zones unless they were guaranteed by the government. Hull declared, "If the gasoline mentioned by your association is indeed being transported to the Italian side, then the government cannot guarantee the safety of the sailors, because the President has made it clear that any national who voluntarily trades with belligerent nations assumes all risks." The freighter Oregon, because the gasoline it carries is being transported to East Africa, now has no hope of setting sail due to Hull's statement. However, it was later learned that the sailors on the ship had accepted a 50% bonus, and the company had also taken out life insurance for the sailors, so the ship can sail to the Far East tonight. (National Telegram, 19th)

Roosevelt Advocates International Cooperation to Eliminate Trade Barriers 42

Former Philippine Governor Delivers Speech: China Awakens Like a Giant from a Dream, Market Development Has Unlimited Prospects

Hot Springs, Texas, USA. The National Foreign Trade Council recently held a meeting here. President Roosevelt sent a letter stating, "The constructive work of creating peace requires a sound and stable economic foundation and free commerce." Today, international trade is not only suffocated by prohibitive tariffs, but also hindered by import quota systems and other restrictions. We cannot take action alone on this issue. We should cooperate with various countries to reduce excessive restrictions and rebuild commercial relations on a fairer basis. Foreign markets must be restored before domestic prosperity can be expected. (Havas, 19th)

Houston. At the annual meeting of the National Foreign Trade Council held here today, former Governor of the Philippines Forbes said that a market with great potential is currently developing in China, but other countries are taking the opportunity to enjoy it. He also said that China is like a giant who has been sleeping for a long time, and is now gradually moving and showing signs of awakening. The agent of the National Bank of Mexico, Mr. Glenn, told the audience about the relationship between silver and Mexican trade, saying that the United States should purchase Mexican silver at the price of purchasing domestic silver, and Mexico, in return, can greatly reduce or exempt import duties on certain American goods, so that both parties can benefit. The President of the Council, Thomas, advocated sending an economic delegation to the Latin American countries within a few months, saying that expanding trade in this area would be very beneficial. (Reuters, 19th)

The Issue of American Protection After Philippine Independence 43

Internal Disagreement

(Washington) Democratic Senator King declared today that the United States should bear the moral responsibility of protecting the Philippines. American officials today disagreed on this issue. Most officials said that the U.S. responsibility to the Philippines will end when the Philippines becomes fully independent in 1946. Other officials only agreed with part of King's claim, but said that future circumstances would be extremely important in determining whether the United States sends troops to assist the Philippines. Observers said that the current U.S. is permeated with a spirit of non-intervention, which will naturally oppose this assistance, but as time passes, this public opinion may change. Within ten years after the establishment of the Philippine autonomous government, the United States will be responsible for the Philippines. People here generally believe that the Philippine national defense problem is still in its infancy. The suggestions of the former American Chief of Staff, now the American Military Commissioner to the Philippines, General MacArthur, will most influence the American attitude towards the Philippines after complete independence. (National News Agency, 19th)

London Naval Conference 44

Scheduled to Open on the Sixth of Next Month, Candidates for the U.S. Delegation

(London) Although the date of the naval conference has not yet been officially announced, Reuters has learned that the conference will likely open on the morning of December 6th in the Foreign Office's "Locarno Room," or on Friday evening with a ceremony personally opened by the British King. That evening, the British government will hold a formal banquet at St. James's Palace to await the representatives of various countries, which will be the formal opening ceremony of this conference. On Saturday and Sunday, the representatives will enjoy themselves in the countryside. On Monday, the conference will begin its serious work at Clarence House on Pall Mall in the Westminster district. The building was originally a place for business gatherings, but has recently been renovated into a conference center. (Reuters, 20th)

(Washington) The U.S. representatives to the London Naval Conference were announced today by President Roosevelt, namely Davis, Undersecretary of State who attended the 1932 Naval Conference, Phelps, and Stanley, Director of Naval Deployments. It is said that after attending the conference and becoming familiar with all the circumstances, Mr. Phelps will return to the United States to serve as a liaison officer between the State Department and the London Naval Representative. Mr. Davis will be the chief representative, and the date of departure has not yet been determined. (National Telegram, 19th)

(New York) Norman Davis, the former representative of the U.S. government in London and Geneva, will now lead the U.S. delegation to the London Naval Conference. President Roosevelt also appointed Deputy Undersecretary of State Phillips and Major General Standley as U.S. representatives. President Roosevelt explained the reason for appointing Mr. Phillips as a representative today, saying that it would allow Mr. Phillips to become familiar with the circumstances of the naval conference and then return home to serve as a liaison for the naval conference. President Roosevelt also told reporters that the United States opposes a navy that is even more expensive than today's navy. (Reuters, 19th)

Assassination of the King of Yugoslavia Case - Trial of Three Accomplices Begins 49

Conflict Between Defendant's Lawyer and Judge

Aix-en-Provence, France. Three Croats accused of being involved in the assassination in Marseille last year were brought to court today. When the defendant's lawyer, Desmond, began his defense, a messenger handed a sealed envelope to the jurors. The defendant's lawyer, Desmond, immediately demanded that its contents be announced. The two sides then began to argue, and the trial was temporarily suspended. When the trial resumed shortly afterwards, a representative of the jurors stated that the jurors had destroyed the contents of the envelope. Later it was learned that the envelope contained a newspaper, which claimed that the weapon used by terrorists to kill the King of Yugoslavia Alexander and French Foreign Minister Barthou was supplied by Italy. When the trial resumed in the afternoon, the defendant's lawyer, Desmond, had a major conflict with the judge and the prosecutor, engaging in a heated exchange of words. The judge finally ordered that Desmond be removed from the list of lawyers. Desmond was later driven out of court by bailiffs, and the case was adjourned until tomorrow for retrial. The defendants are now threatening to go on a hunger strike if Desmond is not recalled. (Reuters, 19th)

Simple Life Insurance to Be Launched in Nanjing, Hankou, and Shanghai at the Beginning of Next Month 65

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Transportation is launching simple life insurance, which is scheduled to be launched on December 1st by the savings and remittance bureaus in Shanghai, Nanjing, and Hankou. He Zongyan, the manager of the Nanjing Savings and Remittance Bureau, went to Shanghai a few days ago to consult with Director-General Shen Shuyu. According to the discussion, simple life insurance has been implemented in various European countries for some time. Our country is initially establishing it with 500,000 yuan allocated by the Ministry of Transportation as a fund. Various preparation procedures have already been formulated by the head office. The bureau in Nanjing is responsible for handling this matter. Management bureaus in other locations will begin next March and will not be specially organized. In the future, it is planned to recruit a number of solicitors to solicit insurance policies from outside, and subsidies will be given based on their performance. The scope of insurance is divided into two categories: whole life and term life, with the amount of insurance ranging from 50 yuan to 500 yuan. Anyone over the age of twelve can apply for insurance, and the procedures are simple. Those without bad habits or disabilities can apply for insurance. The premiums collected are only about two-fifths of one percent. Those who take out this life insurance policy will have their premiums suspended within a reasonable range if they become disabled, etc., halfway through, and they will still be able to receive the full amount of the premium when it expires. This simple life insurance is quite suitable for the middle class, and it is expected that business will develop rapidly in the future. (Special dispatch on the 20th)

(Hangzhou) The winter labor service in Zhejiang, the Hangzhou, Haiyan, Xiaoshan, and Shaoxing seawall projects began today. The preparation of water conservancy projects in Hangzhou City, Hangzhou County, Haiyan, Haiyan County, Yuhang, Fuyang, and Shengxian counties has been completed and will be implemented within the week. Operations in Shouchang, Longyou, Qu County, Jiangshan, and Jiande counties will begin at the beginning of next month. Road construction will be slightly delayed. Zhang Zili, the director of the office, went to Hangzhou-Haiyan seawall this morning for inspection, and went to Jiaxing to convene the county magistrates of Hai, Chong, Tong, and Shan to discuss road conscription. He returned to the province in the evening. (Special dispatch on the 20th)

Current Financial Situation in Guangxi Province 74

The Price of Silver Plummets, and Guangxi Banknotes Rise in Value Invisibly. Commercial Exchanges Have Changed to Using Guangxi Banknotes for Transactions

Guangzhou correspondence: Since the central government and Guangdong province promulgated currency management measures, silver coins have lost their utility as currency. Silver is purchased by legal currency agencies. All places that usually use silver coins are affected. In Guangxi province, Guangdong silver dollars were commonly used in the past. The value of silver dollars was higher than that of Guangxi province's banknotes. Since Guangdong changed to using silver dollar notes as legal currency, the value of Guangdong silver dollars circulating in Wuzhou, Guangxi province, has fallen sharply. At the same time, the value of Guangxi province banknotes has risen sharply. Previously, 100 Guangdong silver dollars were worth 120 Guangxi banknotes. Since the 7th of this month, they are only worth 107 yuan. As for silver dollars, which were usually worth 140 Guangxi banknotes per 100 yuan, are now only worth 120 yuan. Guangxi merchants, because the central government and Guangdong province abolished silver dollars, have been selling silver dollars in large quantities in recent days, so the financial situation has changed greatly for a time. Merchants who stored silver coins have suffered heavy losses. The salt market and yarn market both suspended trading. The Wuzhou Post Office has also recently taken the central government's legal currency as the standard, and announced that one postal currency equals 1.45 silver dollars, and one postal currency equals 250 copper coins. According to news from Guangdong Bank, although Guangxi has not actually promulgated the whole province's currency control measures, the Guangxi banknotes issued by Guangxi Bank have long been invisibly designated as Guangxi's legal currency. Yesterday, the Guangxi Provincial Government also ordered the Wuzhou Guangxi Bank and the Wuxian County Government to inform the Wuzhou Chamber of Commerce that all silver transactions in the market will be changed to Guangxi banknotes for trading. Furthermore, the silver dollar treasury bonds issued by the Guangxi Provincial Government may also be recalled in the future to unify the legal currency. Therefore, the reform of the currency system in Guangxi Province is proceeding smoothly, but the export of silver from the province cannot but be strictly prohibited. Yesterday, the Guangxi Provincial Government ordered all counties and agencies to completely prohibit the export of silver, silver utensils, and silver ingots from the province. Those who smuggle or harbor smugglers will be punished by death in accordance with the Emergency Law for Punishing Acts Endangering the Republic of China. The original order is as follows: "It is hereby noted that our country is a silver standard country. Recently, since the price of silver has risen sharply, silver has been flowing out continuously, financial resources have been exhausted, and industry and commerce have been declining. If this continues without seeking remedies, the consequences will be dire. Recently, the central government resolutely promulgated currency management measures, which is an urgent measure to save the national economic crisis. All provinces have followed the orders after receiving them, and restrictions on the export of silver and all silver goods are strictly enforced. Under the same circumstances in this province, we should quickly plan good policies to preserve the existing silver. All silver and silver utensils such as silver ingots are completely prohibited from being transported out of the province. They are still allowed to circulate within the province. Those who smuggle or harbor smugglers shall be punished by death in accordance with the Emergency Law for Punishing Acts Endangering the Republic of China. All county bureaus along the border should strictly investigate and deal with them. If there are any omissions, the county bureau chiefs shall be held responsible. All anti-smuggling, coast guard, and customs police teams must still be responsible for assisting in the investigation to prevent negligence. All should comply with the above and be recorded by each county bureau and chamber of commerce for public notice" (November 15th)

Hubei Province Appeals to the Central Government to Allocate 5 Million for Industrial Relief 75

The Central Government Has Already Allocated 500,000 in Relief Funds

Hankou Correspondence: Since Hubei Province suffered an unprecedented flood in July, the authorities immediately decided to treat the symptoms with emergency relief and agricultural relief, and treat the root cause with industrial relief. The opinions of the central and local governments are consistent, but because the relief funds are small, the work to treat the root cause is just empty talk. Now, as the weather turns cold and the year ends, the victims are suffering from hunger and cold, and deaths are following one another. If construction is not started again, it may affect public security and cause a major disaster. This is an extremely serious problem that must be addressed. It is noted that the central government has allocated seven batches of relief funds to Hubei Province this year, totaling 10,500 yuan for the first batch, 10,000 yuan for the second batch, 15,000 yuan for the third batch, 5,000 yuan for the fourth batch, 10,000 yuan for the fifth batch, 5,000 yuan for the sixth batch, and 6,000 yuan for the seventh batch, plus 300,000 yuan allocated for disaster relief reserves, totaling 511,500 yuan. In addition, 150,000 yuan was received from the Shanghai fundraising for the inter-provincial flood relief association. Except for the sixth and seventh relief funds and the reserves allocated by the central government, all the funds have been distributed to various counties, but it is still felt that it is not enough. The industrial relief requires even more funds. The provincial government previously requested the central government to allocate 5 million yuan for industrial funds, which was originally the lowest estimate. Now it is heard that the central government can only raise 1 million yuan, which is a huge difference, making it difficult to start construction as scheduled. The provincial government and the Flood Relief General Association specially telegraphed President Wang and Minister Kong yesterday as the most urgent appeal. The provincial government's telegram stated, "To President Wang of the Nanjing Executive Yuan, Minister Kong of the Ministry of Finance, We are in receipt of the telegram from the secretariat of the Economic Commission, stating that (1) the Zhongxiang Sisi engineering dam blocking project and breach, (2) the Jianghan main dike, (3) the civil dike and other projects in Hubei Province will require funding, spring [projected amount], which has been approved by this committee, allowing the central and local governments to each bear 1 million yuan, and the remaining 3 million yuan has been submitted to the Executive Yuan for approval, and the Ministry of Finance has been approved to find ways to raise funds. After suffering a catastrophic disaster in this province, the people are in dire straits, and the dikes and embankments have been destroyed. Without allocating huge funds to carry out industrial relief, and using industrial relief to repair the dikes and embankments, there is no way to save the remaining people and relieve the harm. After repeated estimates and reports of the required number of funds, we have explicitly requested that they be raised and allocated quickly. Now, according to the previous reason, the central government will only allow the allocation of 1 million for industrial relief in this province, which is a huge difference from the original estimated number and is really insufficient for distribution. Now the weather is cold, and it is also the time of emergency winter defense. If industrial relief is delayed again, the victims will die of hunger and cold, and it is feared that major changes will occur in the local situation. The situation is extremely urgent. For the sake of disaster relief and security, we can only appeal to increase the allocation according to the number requested in the previous telegram."

Exchange Rates

The exchange rate against the US dollar fell slightly this morning, while the French exchange rate remained largely unchanged. Most merchants are standing by to wait for the meeting of the International Rubber Restriction Committee on December 3.

Public utility stocks were firm again, with New York Gas being the strongest, and International Telephone and Telegraph stocks were also strong. Although steel stocks and auto stocks rose in opening prices, they fell below yesterday's closing prices due to profit-taking. Anhui Flood Relief Association Provides Relief to Disaster Victims in Various Counties 77

Divided into First, Second, and Third Classes, Distribution Will Begin Immediately

Wuhu Correspondence: The Anhui Flood Relief Association believes that during the winter season, it is necessary to actively carry out relief efforts for the flood victims. Based on the disaster reports from various counties, the reports have been submitted for review. Last Saturday, Committee Member Guo entrusted someone to review the disaster reports from Dongliu, Qianshan, Fanchang, Tongling, Guichi, Huaining, Taihu, Tongcheng, Wangjiang, Susong, Zhixian, Wuwei, He County, Wuhu, and Dangtu counties. As a result of the review, except for Wangjiang, Susong, and Zhixian counties, which have already been entrusted to the Shanghai Flood Relief Association to distribute on their behalf, the disaster situation in the other eleven counties of Huai and Tong, except for Qianshan, which was lightly flooded and not considered a disaster, is not included in the list. The disaster-stricken counties are classified according to the size of the breach range, the width of the submerged fields, and the number of disaster-stricken households. The opinions are as follows: (1) In Huaining, Tongcheng, Fanchang, and Tongling counties, more than 40 or 50 breaches have occurred in each district, the population of the disaster-stricken areas ranges from 8,000 or 9,000 to over 30,000 or 40,000, and the flooded fields are over 20,000 or 30,000 mu. They should be listed as first class. (2) In Dangtu, Wuhu, Wuwei, Taihu, and Guichi counties, there are more than 10 breaches in each district, the population of the disaster-stricken areas ranges from tens of thousands to over 30,000, and the flooded fields total more than 40,000 or 50,000 mu. They should be listed as second class. (3) In He County and Dongliu County, there are only three or four breaches in each district, or they are not breaches but flooded by water intrusion, with only six or seven districts. According to the number of affected households and submerged fields listed in the report, although the figures are said to be large on paper, judging from the facts, there are very few breaches in the county. Subtracting the repair of the breach engineering, the losses are small and the disaster is light. They should be listed as third class. The above-listed three classes of counties and districts, the distribution of relief funds should be determined by the general meeting. The fifth standing committee meeting of the association decided to allocate 2,500 yuan to each first-class county, 2,000 yuan to each second-class county, and 1,500 yuan to each third-class county. Personnel will be dispatched to distribute the funds to the respective counties in the near future. (19th)

The Remnant Bandits in Jing County, Anhui, are Being Suppressed 78

Wuhu Correspondence: In the northeastern townships of Jing County, southern Anhui, since the remnant bandits captured Maolin Village last year, they have been entrenched in the deep mountains of Ding Cao Erxi in the eastern townships, appearing and disappearing unpredictably. They have kidnapped about 100 people and disrupted the area for nearly a year, causing great harm to the people in the northeastern townships. People are wary within a few miles of leaving the northeastern gates of Jing City. A rumor about an attack on the city spread last month, and the chamber of commerce telegraphed the province for reinforcements. The northern townships also sent representatives to the province to petition. On the night of the 10th of this month, during a heavy rain, more than 200 remnant bandits washed and looted Chitan Town, Linhe in the northern townships, burning down more than 20 civilian houses and kidnapping about a dozen people, all of whom were store owners. At that time, Wang, the deputy commander of the security team stationed in the city, led a team to suppress them fiercely. After about four hours, the bandits fled. About thirty or forty people from both sides died. On the evening of the 12th, at 10 PM, Commissioner Zeng of Xuan City, Deputy Commander Long of the Security Forces, and Commander Xu of the Fifth Regiment arrived in Jing and decided to set up a temporary bandit suppression headquarters. Long will be stationed there permanently to command. The next afternoon, Commander Shi of the Eleventh Route Army led more than 300 people from Shi Dai to arrive in the city, and the people's hearts were slightly settled. They will set off in the near future to search and suppress the northeastern townships, vowing to eliminate them before stopping.

Completion of Boundary Demarcation Between Hubei, Anhui, and Jiangxi Provinces, and Establishment of Two New Counties 79

Establishment of Binjiang County Between Xun and Huang, Jurisdiction Yet to be Determined; Anhui to Establish Yuexi County, Part of Hubei to be Placed Under Its Jurisdiction

Hankou Correspondence: The governments of Hubei, Anhui, and Jiangxi provinces, previously acting on central government orders, were required to re-demarcate the boundaries of counties in the border regions. They jointly dispatched personnel to Xun to conduct on-site surveys and hold boundary demarcation meetings in Xun. Special attention was paid to facilitating administration and water conservancy construction. This work has now been completed. The Hubei Provincial Boundary Survey Committee has returned to Hubei from Xun to report on its mission. It is reported that, as a result of consultations between the representatives of the three provinces, slight changes were made to the original provincial boundaries. It is proposed to separate the area west of Konglong Town, belonging to Huangmei County, extending east to Chenjiaying, and the Fengyi and Feng'er townships, belonging to Jiujiang in Jiangxi, to establish a new county, to be named Binjiang County. Detailed plans are currently being jointly drafted by the authorities of the three provinces. Which province it will belong to in the future will be determined by the central government. However, this boundary demarcation is of great importance to the management of the Mahua Embankment, which is shared by the three provinces. The embankment traverses the three provinces, making it difficult to coordinate repairs in peacetime and emergency reinforcement in times of crisis, often leading to major disasters. It would be better to place it under the responsibility of one province. As for which province it will belong to in the future, based on the past division of expenses, Hubei Province has borne 56%, Anhui Province 31%, and Jiangxi Province 13%. Therefore, it can be predicted that it will be assigned to Hubei Province. In addition, the borders of Shucheng, Huoshan, Qianshan, and Taihu counties in Anhui province are intricately intertwined with those of Yingshan County in Hubei province. The chairman of Anhui Province, Liu Zhenhua, specially consulted with the chairman of Hubei Province, Zhang Qun, to establish a new county in the overlapping areas of these counties, to be named Yuexi. This has been submitted to the Chairman's Headquarters for approval. The Hubei Provincial Government, considering that part of the county's territory is within its own province, needed to send a senior official to investigate and determine its feasibility. Committee member Fan Xiji was dispatched to conduct an on-site survey and discuss everything with Liu. He deemed it feasible. Today, a telegram was sent from Anhui to the Secretary-General of the Provincial Government, Lu Zhu, reporting the progress: "Wuchang Provincial Government, Secretary-General Lu Dian Sheng brother, the case of adding a new county in the border area of Ying, Huo, Shu, Qian, and Tai has been properly planned by the Anhui Provincial Government. The part related to Hubei Province only involves a few Bao in the Taojiahe, Xiaojiahe, and Zhanjiahe area of the third district of Ying, which need to be placed under the jurisdiction of the newly established Yuexi County. After investigation, this plan is very unreasonable. From the perspective of terrain, the administrative area is more complete. In terms of public security, Taojiahe is far from Ying and the government's orders are difficult to reach, making it easy for bandits to occupy. Based on the above reasons, I have fully accepted the methods proposed by the Anhui Provincial Government. Furthermore, Anhui Province has been preparing for the establishment of the new county for a long time. At a time when bandits are roaming, in order to save time and quickly achieve success, I am sending the draft presentation and the official document of consultation at the same time to Hubei. Please forward them to the chairman after arrival and submit them for discussion and decision quickly. Brother Fan Xiji bows." (17th)

Hu Wenhu Visits Xiamen 80

Xiamen Correspondence: Hu Wenhu of the Central Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission, accompanied by You Fanwu and Ye Guisong, arrived in Xiamen on the Cantonese-Shanghai plane "Fujian" at about 1:00 PM on the 12th. Many shops hung flags to welcome him. From the Zhongshan Pier to the Municipal Party Headquarters, a total of three ceremonial arches were erected. In the afternoon, at 1:00 PM, the Shanghai plane departed from Fuzhou. Representatives of various agencies, schools, and organizations lined up from the Narcissus Pier to Zhongshan Road. At 1:10 PM, Chen Wenlin, Director of the Naval Aviation Department, flew the Jiangpeng training aircraft around the river. Seeing the "Fujian" plane flying from the north, the welcomers boarded an electric boat to the seaplane station. Hu immediately shook hands with Chen Lianfen, Special Commissioner of Party Affairs, Tu Chao, Secretary-General of the Municipal Government, Liu Jingxiao, Representative of the Fortress Headquarters, Shen Jinkang, Director of the Public Security Bureau, Wang Chengzhang, Commander of the Second Marine Police Brigade, Wang Rulin, Director of the Caishan Special Zone, and Hu Zizhou, President of the Xingguang Daily, at the floating station. He then boarded an electric boat of the Fortress Headquarters and landed at the Narcissus Pier, and immediately took a car with Chen Lianfen and others to the Municipal Party Headquarters. After arriving at the Municipal Party Headquarters, he first went upstairs to the reception room for a short rest at 2:10 PM. At 2:00 PM, he went to the auditorium downstairs to attend the welcome meeting of various circles. More than 2,000 representatives from agencies, schools, and organizations participated. After the meeting started, Chairman Chen Lianfen delivered a welcome speech, followed by Hu's reply, which was narrated by Gu Jinqing, an overseas Chinese from Yangon. Ministry of Finance Plans to Establish Silver Depositories in Shanghai, Hankou, Tianjin, and Guangzhou 81

Silver to be Kept by Branches of the Issuance Reserve Fund Committee; Situation in Wuhan Stabilizes, Market Returns to Normal

Hankou Correspondence: It has been nearly half a month since Wuhan implemented currency reform according to orders. The disturbances in the market have largely subsided. The two major problems of inevitable stagnation in copper coin redemption and rising commodity prices have now become a thing of the past. Initially, copper coins were hoarded by unscrupulous merchants, but the government repeatedly issued orders, making it difficult to hoard. In addition, the legal exchange rate was set at six strings of copper coins for one legal tender yuan, preventing unscrupulous merchants from manipulating the market. The copper coins gradually flowed out and retail trade was able to resume as usual. In order to alleviate the situation in the market, the provincial government decided to issue copper coin notes with a total value of one million strings. However, as the copper coin situation returned to normal, the issue was reduced to one hundred thousand strings, and the printing was agreed upon. However, in the past few days, copper coins have become even looser, and the issuance is planned to be temporarily suspended. As for the commodity price problem, after officials and merchants discussed forming a Commodity Price Evaluation Committee, and after the provincial government, municipal government, and garrison headquarters issued announcements to suppress high prices, the rising trend finally stabilized. Currently, except for daily necessities, which are still higher than before, most other items have fallen to normal prices. Although the Commodity Price Evaluation Committee has not been established, representatives from various agencies have already been appointed, and Wang Kaihua, Section Chief of the Civil Affairs Department, has been designated as a standing committee member. Recently, as commodity prices have gradually stabilized, there is also a proposal to temporarily suspend its establishment. Currently, the legal tender issued by the Big Three banks accounts for the majority of currency circulating in Wuhan, with the rest being banknotes issued by various banks. Silver has disappeared. The Big Three banks and various banks have received a total of more than 12.57 million yuan in cash so far. According to financial sources, in order to gain the trust of the people, the Ministry of Finance has decided not to concentrate the cash received in one place, but to establish four major depositories in Shanghai, Hankou, Tianjin, and Guangzhou, with each branch of the Issuance Reserve Fund Management Committee responsible for safekeeping. The large amount of cash in Wuhan will also be transferred to the branch of the Issuance Reserve Management Committee and will no longer be shipped abroad. It is also reported that since receiving an urgent order from the Ministry of Finance, the Jianghan Customs has prohibited the import and export of cash, so no handover has been received. (17th)

Guangdong Province: Demand for Legal Tender Exceeds Supply 82

Printing Existing Silver Dollar Notes and Converting Them into Silver Dime Legal Tender; Regulations of the Issuance Reserve Management Committee Passed

Guangzhou Correspondence: Since Guangdong Province announced the management of currency and the collection of hard currency with legal tender, depositors of silver dimes in various places have been flocking to the Provincial Bank to exchange silver for legal tender. As a result, the Provincial Bank had received 15 million yuan in silver dimes as of the 14th. The dime notes of legal tender printed by the Provincial Bank are about to be exhausted, so it has had to issue existing silver dollar notes as dime notes of legal tender. In the past few days, it has stamped the printed one-yuan and ten-yuan silver dollar notes with the words "for silver dime note use" and issued them with signatures. The Finance Department has officially announced that the silver dollar notes stamped as silver dime notes by the Provincial Bank are considered legal tender, and should be used in the same way as one-yuan, five-yuan, ten-yuan, and one-hundred-yuan silver dime legal tender, whether for tax collection or market transactions. Furthermore, the Provincial Bank has recently limited the exchange of silver for legal tender, as the demand for silver dime notes exceeds the supply. Those with less than 200 yuan are allowed to exchange for one-yuan, five-yuan, and ten-yuan dime notes. Those with 200 to 1,000 yuan can exchange for 100-yuan dime notes. Those with more than 1,000 yuan need to fill out a form and register for exchange. To prevent unscrupulous merchants from buying silver, non-designated silver shops are not allowed to privately collect silver, and violators will be severely punished. As for various cities and towns in the province, they are now buying silver with dime notes. Places such as Jiangmen, Foshan, Shilong, and Chencun have been buying and transporting dime notes to the province for storage in recent days. As for Shantou, which usually uses silver dollars, the Finance Department has specially formulated measures. All official payments in Shantou are settled in dime notes, still calculated by adding 3% to the locality and 2% to the note, plus one yuan for water. The Shantou Branch of the Guangdong Provincial Bank has announced the above measures to merchants and residents.

Since the Provincial Bank started buying silver, it has reached 20 million yuan. It will continue to collect silver in the future. There should be a responsible agency for the custody of large sums of reserves. The Provincial Government held a special meeting on the morning of the 13th to discuss the organizational rules of the Guangdong Legal Tender Issuance Reserve Management Committee, which were immediately revised and passed. The original text is as follows: Article 1: The Guangdong Provincial Government specially establishes the Legal Tender Issuance Reserve Committee to consolidate the credit of legal tender. Article 2: The Legal Tender Issuance Reserve Management Committee, acting on the orders of the Guangdong Provincial Government, shall be responsible for the custody of the reserve fund and the review of the issuance amount of legal tender. Article 3: The amount of legal tender issued shall be based on the price index and the principle of matching supply and demand. Article 4: The Legal Tender Issuance Reserve Management Committee shall be composed of the following personnel: 1. Two representatives from the Guangdong Provincial Chamber of Commerce Federation; 2. Two representatives from the Guangzhou Municipal Chamber of Commerce; 3. One representative from the Shantou Municipal Chamber of Commerce; 4. One representative from the Haikou Municipal Chamber of Commerce; 5. One representative from the Jiangmen Municipal Chamber of Commerce; 6. Two representatives from the Guangzhou Bankers Association; 7. One representative each from the Guangzhou Silver Association and Zhongxintang; 8. The President and Vice President of the Guangdong Provincial Bank; 9. The President of the Guangzhou Municipal Bank; 10. One representative from the Guangdong Provincial Finance Department; 11. One to three financial leaders or experts selected by the Guangdong Provincial Government, and those with social prestige. Article 5: The Legal Tender Issuance Reserve Management Committee shall have five standing committee members. In addition to the representative from the Guangdong Provincial Finance Department and the President of the Guangdong Provincial Bank serving as standing committee members, the remaining three shall be elected from the representatives sent by each committee member organization. Article 6: The Legal Tender Issuance Reserve Management Committee may hire economic experts as consultants and may establish various specialized committees. Article 7: The reserve fund is limited to the following: 1. Original silver coins; 2. Raw gold and silver; 3. Foreign silver coins; 4. Marketable securities. Article 8: When the Guangdong Provincial Bank issues legal tender, it shall submit the issuance amount along with the reserve fund to the Legal Tender Issuance Reserve Management Committee for review, and then submit it to the Guangdong Provincial Government for approval and issuance. Article 9: The Legal Tender Issuance Reserve Management Committee is subject to the supervision of the Guangdong Provincial Assembly. The Guangdong Provincial Assembly shall send auditors to the Legal Tender Issuance Reserve Management Committee at any time to check the reserve fund, and shall publicly announce and report the issuance amount and reserve amount separately to the Guangdong Provincial Government for verification and filing on a monthly basis. Article 10: The Issuance Reserve Committee may employ personnel to handle matters in different sections. Article 11: The detailed rules of the Issuance Reserve Management Committee shall be drafted by the committee and submitted to the Guangdong Provincial Government for approval. Article 12: These regulations shall be implemented after being submitted to the Southwest Political Affairs Committee for review and filing. (November 14th)

Songjiang

Lianshui Refugees Pass Through Songjiang Seeking Food

Recently, 132 refugees from Renhang Township, Fourth District, Lianshui County, carrying the old and supporting the young, led by the people's representative Li Hecai, sought food along the way, describing the tragic situation of the famine. They have arrived in the territory of the Third Garrison of this port via Tianmashan. The garrison considered that during the winter defense period, the large number of people was related to public security and did not allow them to stay. After raising funds and providing rations, the group of refugees proceeded towards Fengjing.

Wuxi

Implementation of Compulsory Literacy Education

The case of compulsory literacy education in Wuxi was initiated by Zang Fogen, the former Director of the Education Bureau. According to the latest household registration survey, the total population of the county is more than one million, and it is estimated that half of them, 500,000, are illiterate. Among them, middle-aged illiterate people between the ages of 16 and 45 account for more than 100,000. According to the provincial order, the principle is that at least one person per household should attend school. There are a total of 200,000 households in the county, and 100,000 people must attend school. Assuming 50 students per school, 4,000 schools should be established, to be operated in three phases. Each phase will establish 1,330 schools. According to the Baojia system, each small Bao will set up a civil school or a civil literacy class, and each large Bao will run a civil school or a civil literacy class every two Baos. Divided into three phases, each phase can eliminate illiteracy for 66,600 people. Each school will be subsidized 30 yuan for books and other expenses. The first phase should cost 40,000 yuan. The above plan has been submitted to the Education Department for modification and approval, and the current Director Hui Meishan has been ordered by the County Government to implement it conscientiously. Wu Xilin, Yan Yangdou, and Gu Jingcun have been appointed as members of the public literacy reader review committee to determine the textbooks. The first phase has been decided to be implemented within this month.

Jiading

Buying Hard Currency Sent to County for Investigation

Xu Xingzhong, who has been working in a rice shop in Yangshupu, Shanghai, near Huichun Tangerine in Nanmen, returned to Jiading on the 17th. He contacted various shops in the city to exchange legal tender for hard currency. Someone secretly reported him to the Zhouqiao Patrol Station. The police immediately investigated and saw him discussing prices with someone in a meat shop on Dongdajie. They immediately arrested him and sent him to the County Public Security Bureau. They found 211 yuan of legal tender and 9 yuan of hard currency on his person. Under interrogation by Section Chief Zhu, Xu initially denied it, claiming that the silver coins he carried were brought to Shanghai by a neighbor, Wang [omitted]. After investigation, it was found that Wang did not entrust him. It was also learned that Xu had exchanged legal tender for hard currency with Wang Bingyi of Zhenchangqian North-South Goods Store in Nan [omitted], ten [omitted] for hard currency [omitted]. Wang was summoned to confront him. Wang then admitted that he had taken the exchange to Shanghai to make a profit. He also admitted that he had done it before, so someone would come to exchange with him after he went to Shanghai. The Public Security Bureau sent the case to the County Government for judicial investigation along with the suspect Wang.

Yangzhou

Majiaqiao Robbery Case to be Pronounced

Wang Chunbo and Zhou Fakuan, farmers from Majiaqiao, Xiannv Town, Fourth District of the county, were robbed on the night of September 23 last year. The case was reported to the county, and the county ordered the case to be solved. The Public Security Reconnaissance Team subsequently arrested four suspects, Tao Haicheng, Di Xuezheng, Xu Huaiguo, and Tao Wu, in the Xiannv Temple area. They were sent to the court. After investigation by the Prosecutor's Office, the Criminal Court conducted several interrogations. The 19th was another court date. The victims and the witness Gu Jinshan attended the court to testify. The defendants were also brought to the court from prison. The defendants were defended by lawyer Dai Tianqiu. The court session began at 10:00 AM, presided over by Judge Xu. The result was an announcement that the debate was over and the sentence would be pronounced on the 25th of this month.

It is urgent to conduct on-site investigations to improve the situation. Yesterday, it specially dispatched technician Lu Chi to conduct detailed investigations and inspections. He will first inspect Huangyan, Yongjia, and [omitted] counties, as well as the situation of the Huangyan County Government cooperating with the Jinling University Agricultural College to conduct citrus storage experiments.

Nanjing

Xiaobao Promotes Simple Words and Phrases

Wang Zhiyuan, Secretary-General of the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission, is usually enthusiastic about public education. He promoted literacy campaigns in Guangdong in the past. In 1930, he founded the Qianzi Daily in Shanghai, using simple characters to popularize education, which was very effective. Recently, in order to implement this idea, Wang specially founded Xiaobao in Nanjing, publishing one sheet a day, with a novel format, fast and accurate news, and simple content, encompassing everything. It can be said to be a unique color in the news industry. The newspaper has now been published and sells very well. Readers generally enjoy subscribing to it because its words and phrases are simple. The newspaper uses only 1,500 root characters, which are determined to be the most common in daily life. All complex characters are replaced by root characters, so those who have studied for three months and know more than 1,000 characters can read about world affairs.

Bandits Rob Two Shops in Jingyou Town

In Jingyou Town, Fourth District of Xiaoshan County, on the night of the 15th, when the wind and rain were heavy, more than a dozen bandits suddenly came, speaking with a local accent and carrying earthen guns. They first went to the Fuxing North-South Goods Store, broke down the doors and entered, looting all the cash, clothes, bedding, etc. of the partners, causing a loss of more than 200 yuan. Then they went to the Hengyu Beijing Goods Store to rob, taking away all the coppers, socks, towels, etc., worth more than 80 yuan in total. It is reported that they fled towards Tianle Township, Shaoxing County at dawn.

Impressions of a Trip to Guangxi (Continued) 83

— Qian Hua

Fifthly, the tragic phenomenon of national subjugation is the most shocking, and it can never be erased. When this reporter arrived in Longzhou, I visited Zhennanguan to see the historical relics of our country's victory over the French. Looking at the past and present, the country is in trouble and foreign enemies are pressing in. It's truly a mix of laughter and tears. This reporter temporarily waited for a passport to go abroad, left Zhennanguan, entered Annam, and arrived at Lang Son, where the Black Flag Army led by Liu Yongfu was stationed. Military victory led to peaceful negotiations, a heartbreaking history, unbearable to recall. Today, the mountains and rivers remain the same, but the scenery is completely different. Everywhere there are small French-style houses, asphalt roads, wide and neat streets, and trees lining the roads. There are trains and highways, and transportation is extremely convenient. The Annamese people certainly enjoy more material civilization than before their subjugation, but spiritually, they have deep scars. This reporter interviewed a middle-class Annamese family. The house was full of old things, and there were also some scattered calligraphy and paintings. Knowing that I was Chinese, they looked very cordial. When I asked about various situations, they just sighed and shook their heads. The so-called "a belly full of bitterness" was all unspoken. I also visited an Annamese primary school, where the main subjects were taught by the French. Half of each week was devoted to French and the other half to Annamese. The Annamese language originally used Chinese characters, and street names and house numbers were also in Chinese characters. Now, the Annamese language is spelled using the French alphabet. In thirty years, there will be no more Chinese characters in Annam. From this one aspect, the rest can be imagined. There's really no need for this reporter to say more.

Sixthly, Guilin's scenery is the best in the world. All the peaks rise uniquely from the local area. The jade bamboo shoots and Yao ginseng stand tall without end, and the mountains are all hollow, with deep, remote, and peculiar caves. In addition, along the Li River, there are many clear streams and dangerous ravines, creating scenery everywhere that is endless to explore. Besides Beijing and Hangzhou, it has a unique style. It's a pity that it hasn't been developed by human efforts, transportation is obstructed, and facilities are inadequate. There are no ancient temples adorning the mountains, making it difficult for tourists to stay in the mountains and take candlelit night tours. The Guilin authorities have planned to make Guilin a cultural tourism area, but there is no definite funding. This reporter believes that a large sum of money should be allocated, or public bonds should be issued, and a specialized organization should be established to engage in the construction of the tourist area. In the famous scenic spots such as Yangshuo and Liangfeng, more villas and hotels should be built to accommodate distant tourists. Guidebooks and other pamphlets should be widely printed. More clean hostels should also be set up in Guilin city. Pavilions and kiosks should be added to the famous mountains, and wine, food, and tea should be served. Guilin suffers from inconvenient transportation. It takes two days to go from Hong Kong to Wuzhou. From Wuzhou, sailing up the Gui River to Guilin, shallow-water electric boats can reach Pingle in about a day during the summer and autumn when the water rises. After September and October, the water becomes shallow and dries up, and electric boats stop running. Only民boats can travel, which takes more than ten days, which is very troublesome. The Guilin authorities are currently rushing to build a highway from Wuzhou to Pingle, which will be open to traffic next spring. The distance between the two places is 400 li, and it can be reached in one day. From Pingle to Guilin, both by water and land, you can arrive in one day. At that time, it will only take three days from Hong Kong to Guilin, which will be much more convenient. European, American, and Japanese countries pay great attention to tourism management, and the construction of tourist areas is regarded as an investment. They use various publicity methods to attract tourists. For example, famous scenic areas in France, Switzerland, and Japan attract an average of millions or even tens of millions of yuan in tourism investment every year. Our country has not paid attention to this. If the Guilin authorities can invest a little, I am convinced that the annual profit will be better than any other undertaking. Moreover, the prosperity of the market and the promotion of education and culture will be additional side income.

Seventhly, why the capital of Guangxi province is located in Nanning is truly a big question. Historically, since the Ming Dynasty, the capital of Guangxi province has been located in Guilin. In the early years of the Republic of China, because Lu Rongting was from Wuming, about forty or fifty li from Nanning, a general trend of followers advocated moving the provincial capital to Nanning. At the same time, the highway from Nanning to Wuming was built, which was the beginning of the Guangxi highway. But Nanning, in any aspect, does not have the qualifications to be a provincial capital. It has no strengths in landscape or cultural relics. You can't find a place to visit or stay in the whole city. When this reporter was in Nanning, I raised this question and discussed it with them. Those who advocated that the provincial capital be located in Nanning had two major reasons. The first is that the population in southern Guangxi is sparse, all industries are declining, and it is close to the border defense, which is extremely important. If the provincial capital is too far away, it will be difficult to manage the border areas. Nanning is located in the south and is especially close to Longzhou. On the one hand, it can encourage immigration, and at the same time, it can prevent the border defense from being abandoned. The second is that Nanning has been the provincial capital for a long time, and various constructions have taken shape. Once it is moved elsewhere, the material loss will be too great and outweigh the gains. But in this reporter's opinion, precisely because Nanning is too close to the border, it should not be made the provincial capital. If there is an alarm on the border, Longzhou is only 640 li from Nanning, and the enemy can drive straight in, endangering the political center of the two provinces. Therefore, from a military point of view, the provincial capital should be moved to a farther location. As for material losses, it is even less of a problem. Even if Nanning is not the provincial capital, it can still be a major town in the south in terms of commerce. Various constructions are also needed. There is also a point that is most crucial. The area near Nanning is a plain, with no mountains or rivers to visit. Civil servants feel lonely and unhappy in their spare time. Gambling is strictly prohibited, and there is no place to visit, so it becomes boring. Especially for people from other provinces who come to Guangxi to work, after half a year or a year, they are eager to leave, holding the idea of ​​leaving early. Guangxi province relies heavily on talents from other provinces for various undertakings. If talents cannot stay for a long time, it will naturally affect the development of the cause. Therefore, in terms of climate, geography, culture, and scenery, Guilin is the most suitable place to be the capital of Guangxi province. At the same time, the construction of the Guilin tourist area will also be easier to achieve with half the effort due to the political center. The next best choice is Liuzhou. Liuzhou is backed by mountains and faces water, with a majestic terrain, located in the central part of Guangxi, in the middle reaches of the Liujiang River. To the southeast, it goes down to Xiangxun to the Xijiang River, and to the northwest, it goes up the Honghe River to Guizhou. To the south, it connects to Yonglong, and to the north, it goes out of Guiquan. It really has the advantage of controlling the whole province. However, the construction of the provincial capital takes time and money, which is not as good as Guilin's existing scale. Today, the enemy's military aggression starts with air force bombing. Aircraft carriers sail to Qinzhou Bay, which is more than 200 li from Nanning. They can fly back and forth in one hour. In case of an accident, the political center, the place where orders are issued, will be in danger of serious threats. If it is changed to Guilin, it will be about 1,300 li from the coast, which is relatively defensive. This is even more reason to move the provincial capital in terms of foreign relations. Of course, there are not a few people in the ruling authorities of Guangxi province who advocate and support moving the provincial capital, but the military leaders Li Zongren and Bai Chongxi happen to be from Guilin, so they have to avoid the meaning of supporting their hometown and do not express their views. But for the future development of Guangxi province, it is best to move the provincial capital to Guilin.

Eighthly, Guangxi province has been working hard on construction in recent years, and its political achievements are outstanding. The cooperation between the military and the people and the diligent and honest spirit of officials are truly commendable. But there is a point that the Guangxi authorities should pay special attention to, which is the training of middle and lower-level cadres. The leaders of Guangxi province have embraced the attitude of setting an example in governing military and political affairs, so everything is being revived and the achievements are remarkable. However, most of the middle and lower-level cadres under the leaders either do not understand the true doctrine or have a sense of obedience but no creativity. They follow the example and do not know why. The foundation does not seem to be very solid. Therefore, in the future, special attention should be paid to the training of cadre talents, so that the people who work below can thoroughly understand the purpose of the administration, not working for others, but serving for the cause. Then, send the trained cadre talents to the people to train the masses, so that all the people in the province have a sense of self-government and a sense of service, and the achievements of Guangxi's governance can be maintained permanently and continue to progress forever. The lack of understanding of middle and lower-level cadre talents can be proven by many examples. The most obvious is the change of clothing. Many people in Guangxi province, of course, wear gray cloth uniforms as ordered, but after leaving Guangxi province, they change into neat suits and look different. When they come back, they change back into cloth clothes. Even the problem of clothing is so artificial. Of course, they do not understand the cloth clothing doctrine advocated by their leaders. By analogy, it is undeniable that they do not have a sufficient understanding of the main point. (End)

The Beijing-Shanghai Railway Repaid Overdue Interest 87

A total of over 1,160,000 yuan.

The Beijing-Shanghai Railway should pay the 60th installment of interest on the Sino-British Yin Company's road construction loan due on May 18, 1934, which is 69,600 pounds, plus bank commission of 174 pounds, totaling 69,774 pounds. The Accounting Office of the two Railways Administration has converted this amount at an exchange rate of one shilling, two pence and three-eighths of a penny to one yuan, totaling 1,164,922.44 yuan, and paid it to HSBC in full yesterday (November 20) for remittance to London. The 59th installment of interest paid on May 18 of this year was the same amount in pounds, which was converted into 835,070.22 yuan. Due to the Sino-British exchange rate, this installment paid 328,852.22 yuan more.

The original scope is small, and there is a plan to move to Wusong.

According to the Central News Agency, the Ministry of Communications coastal radio stations are dedicated to facilitating marine communications, and have unique functions for ship safety and maritime audio information. In recent years, with the development of various industries, the need for coastal radio stations has been increasing day by day. The Ministry of Communications believes that the original radio stations are insufficient and has instructed them to expand. The office of the radio station was originally located at the Hongqiao Radio Station, while the radio station itself was located at Fenglin Bridge. Because the original scope is small, and expansion is limited by land issues, it is currently being planned. The former International Telecommunications Bureau once built a large-scale broadcasting station in Wusong. After this project was canceled midway, the land in Wusong is quite large, so there is talk of moving the radio station to Wusong.
