Points to Note When Implementing Mental Hygiene Education in Elementary Schools 169

— Zhu Zhen

(1) Introduction

One of the main goals of education is to help children achieve healthy and fulfilling lives. To achieve this goal, schools should modify all their procedures, curricula, methods, management, administrative organization, and physical facilities from a mental hygiene perspective. Schools should first establish a standard to determine whether a child's behavior truly exhibits characteristics of maladjustment. If so, the school should find ways to help these maladjusted children achieve greater social and emotional satisfaction.

The first basic need that schools should satisfy for children is the need for spontaneous expression—an outlet for their energy. Methods of providing this outlet often utilize public group life, in which all activities are based on the children's interests, not on their academic standing. Such methods as handicrafts, music, artistic performances, cooking, photography, and other central activities can be used as early as the third grade of elementary school.

The second basic need that schools should satisfy for children is to enable them to participate in socialized activities. Therefore, the school itself should become a free and democratic society, where children can take on responsibilities such as maintaining school buildings and lawns, planning meeting programs, discussing the order of entry into classrooms or auditoriums, and managing school stores, libraries, or cafeterias. Of course, these responsibilities should not include judging criminals or imposing penalties, as this is contrary to mental hygiene.

The spirit of child socialization is cultivated in group life activities or designs. For example, we can have first-graders set up a post office, second-graders build a playground, and sixth-graders organize labor unions, establish school banks, and distribute all school supplies. In these designs, children can maximize their energy and expression according to their interests.

The third need that schools should satisfy for children is a sense of security. They can achieve this goal through spontaneous expression and participation in social activities, not only at school but also at home, to ensure they always feel safe.

(2) Curriculum

From a mental hygiene perspective, all curricula should include those parts that are truly useful for children's lives. Useless and meaningless parts of the curriculum should be removed. Therefore, the curriculum standards we adopt that are consistent with mental hygiene education should be practical. However, there is another standard: teaching materials that children cannot handle should be provided to them after they mature. Modern schools often neglect children's psychological preparation. Therefore, we should study which teaching materials are suitable for each stage of children's psychological growth.

(3) Management

In the sense of mental hygiene, management includes the training of teachers. Teachers should have knowledge of mental hygiene before teaching children and should constantly pursue it after teaching. Secondly, it includes the spirit of cooperation among teachers. At the same time, the school should give teachers freedom, so that they have creative ideas and are allowed to participate in the planning, research, and organization of the curriculum, and even the opportunity to decide on the school's administrative policies.

(4) Administration

In order to pay attention to children's emotional well-being, the school's administrative organization should abolish the system of failing grades and grade retention. Traditional school administrative systems do not pay attention to this point; they punish students without considering the emotional impact of such punishment. For example, in the Winnetka schools in the United States, students are not given grades or ratings for each subject. On their report cards, only an "S" (Satisfactory) or a negative "-" sign is recorded for schoolwork and conduct. Every extremely stupid or extremely clever child should receive an "S" mark because they believe that the negative sign can easily damage a child's emotions, so their teachers try to minimize the negative signs. Secondly, the method of correcting children's test papers or exams should also be different from the norm. Although the errors and corrections on the papers are all indicated, the element of competition in the class should be absolutely prohibited from being announced.

Therefore, for the sake of children's mental hygiene, the entire administrative organization of the school should be flexible so that the curriculum, methods, and other aspects can be adapted to each child. In addition, physical facilities are also important for children's mental hygiene. Therefore, the school should have reasonable physical facilities for children's creative work and socialized activities. However, this type of equipment does not require a lot of money to purchase, as they are mostly various tools and materials for children's work. Finally, the atmosphere in the classroom should be familial, informal, and arranged to please the eye.

(5) Cultivating Normal Behaviors in Children

We undoubtedly neglect the harmless maladjustments of children. Children who outwardly obey teachers often do not attract the deep attention of teachers. In fact, inside them, there is already a kind of unhappy emotion or the suppression of unsatisfied desires. This kind of internal suppression is more dangerous than the outward behavior that indicates maladjustment. Therefore, this behavior is by no means a child's normal behavior. On the other hand, we always pay close attention to disturbing and rebellious children, and often think that their behavior is abnormal. In fact, the behavior exhibited by such children is normal behavior and is of great value from the perspective of the child's mechanical and emotional growth. Therefore, we hope that elementary school teachers will not use suppression methods exclusively but will allow their emotions to be expressed as much as possible. For example, the Winnetka schools in the United States pay very close attention to this point. They often invite psychiatric experts to observe whether the behavior of children in each classroom is normal to set up methods to remedy the situation. On the teacher side, they are also collecting materials on normal adaptation and maladapted children in each grade to do research, hoping to compile a scale of social and emotional behavior from this material to determine normal child behavior in various stages of maturity.

(6) Conclusion

Mental hygiene is indeed an important issue in elementary schools, but it is unfortunately often neglected by so-called education experts. If we want to solve this problem, relying solely on the strength of principals and teachers is not enough. We are bound to also seek help from psychologists and psychiatrists, so elementary schools should hire such experts to be in charge of guidance. This point is certainly not easy to do in today's Chinese education world, where talent and economy are both lacking, but at least elementary school principals and teachers should have common sense about children's mental hygiene. In this way, even in a passive way, they can achieve considerable results.

Finance Gold Market Turns Dull Again 170

Fluctuations of Only $1.90 in Half a Day, Leisurely Result: Slight Increase of $0.30

The gold market was sluggish again yesterday. There were only fluctuations of $1.90 in the first half of the day. The market situation was mediocre, and people were idle. It was found that at the beginning of the morning, the overseas silver market in both the UK and the US was flat, the forward silver price in Montreaux fell by $0.04 to $0.10. The exchange rate was slightly higher. Spot gold in London rose by 1.5 pence. The off-site preparatory transaction opened higher at $99.60. The Central Bank's listed prices revealed that both the UK and the US were flat, the customs gold unit remained unchanged, and the standard gold price was listed at $1151. The morning opening was slightly higher, but sellers were more active after the opening, and the price immediately went downstream. Major players maintained the price at low levels, and retail investors raised prices one after another. Soon, it rose back to the $60 mark, but many people still sold off at the limit price, making it difficult to break through this level. It was known in advance that the HSBC Bank's listed prices were flat for both the UK and the US. At this time, oil settlements were still strong, and the market situation stabilized for a while. Later, as the bank vigorously blocked forward US dollars, sellers gradually cheered up and the price fell again. Major players maintained the price at low levels, and there were no special changes. There was a slight pull-up. It was predicted that the Indian silver would remain unchanged, and the market situation remained stagnant for quite a long time. Major players once sold gold bars, but there were still many short covering. There was a slight fluctuation at noon, but the result was still stable. Looking ahead, it is difficult to break the dull situation. It is really because the industry is watching and there is a lack of supply. Shen Bao National Goods Weekly

Contributions

Raw Material Price Hikes and the National Goods Issue 188

— Yang An

Since the implementation of the new currency policy, although prices have risen at one point, they have recently been able to return to their original state due to the weakness of purchasing power. However, one of the most painful points for the national goods industry in the past has been the soaring prices of raw materials. These raw material merchants, responding psychologically to the currency reform, believe that it is an excellent opportunity to raise prices, hoard goods and manipulate the market, which puts national goods manufacturers in serious difficulty. Mr. Hu Xiyuan saw this early and earnestly advised raw material merchants not to raise prices too suddenly. The reporter expresses great sympathy. The most difficult thing about rising raw material prices is that it is difficult for small and medium-sized factories. On the one hand, purchasing power has not increased sharply, and they cannot raise selling prices. On the other hand, they have to purchase high-priced raw materials, and the cost suddenly increases. This contradictory environment is indeed the biggest reef for the national goods industry. If this continues, the sales of national goods will inevitably stagnate, and the demand for raw materials will decrease, resulting in a lose-lose situation. Mr. Hu has already expressed his concern. The reporter sincerely hopes that raw material merchants will take a long-term view during this transition period, take the overall situation into consideration, and never embrace selfish and self-interested doctrines, taking the opportunity to profit and sacrificing the lifeblood of national goods. As for national goods manufacturers, they should cooperate sincerely among themselves, unite their peers, purchase raw materials wholesale, and understand the procedures for foreign exchange in order to break the monopoly and deception of middlemen. Then, the difficult environment may have a chance to improve.

The Revision of Legal Tender and National Goods 189

— Wei Bin

On the 4th of this month, the Ministry of Finance stopped using silver coins and changed the banknotes of the Central Bank, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications to legal tender. This was resolutely implemented after research by several economic experts and careful consideration by the financial authorities. There are many benefits. Today, I will briefly describe those related to our national goods industry.

(1) Financial Circulation: In recent years, my country has been affected by the world's economic downturn, coupled with frequent disasters, and the United States has increased the price of silver, and silver is constantly flowing out. Although a countervailing tax is levied, it still cannot be stopped. As a result, my country's silver reserves are decreasing day by day, and the market lacks chips. Although industry and commerce reluctantly survived the four bottoms, seven bottoms, and ten bottoms this year, financial stagnation is becoming increasingly obvious and will inevitably lead to a complete collapse. Now, after the change of legal tender, silver is concentrated, and smuggling can be eliminated. Because silver coins are not in circulation, people will definitely switch to using legal tender. The chips on the market can be increased, and financial circulation will not be as lifeless as before.

(2) Price Increase: In recent years, many national goods factories have been closing down, suspending work, or reducing work due to sluggish sales and inability to turn over funds. After the change to legal tender, various prices have increased considerably, and the rural economy can be revitalized. Then, the sales of national goods can be promoted, and they will not be as lifeless as in the past.

(3) Exchange Control: In recent decades, my country has had trade deficits year after year, and money has flowed out. Even if foreigners do not destroy us politically, the economy is enough to kill us. After the revision of legal tender, international exchange rates are controlled by the Central Bank, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications. On the one hand, exchange rates can be stabilized and will not rise or fall sharply or be manipulated by others. On the other hand, trade controls can be implemented and import and export trade can be adjusted. Then, our weak national goods industry will not be defeated by international capitalism.

Fellow members of the national goods industry, the country has done its job to protect our declining national goods industry. How should we strive to cooperate closely with the banking industry, keep pace, concentrate talents, reduce costs, manufacture excellent products, produce quickly, and manage scientifically? At this critical moment, it is also the last chance for our national goods industry to recover. I hope you will all strive forward.

My dear patriots, everyone is responsible for the rise and fall of the country. There are no intact eggs under an overturned nest. From today onwards, resolve to use national goods. The country's future depends on it.

The New Life Road of the National Goods Industry 190

— Yang An

The economic group's review report of the Fifth National Congress contained a motion that is worth mentioning, that is, the government should earnestly protect the cotton textile industry and eliminate all difficulties. Reducing interest rates on loans and freight is considered to be the key to rescuing the general industry. It is proposed that the congress pass the principle and hand it over to the government to stipulate the statutory interest rate for industrial loans and reduce freight rates, and instruct the competent authorities to handle it. This is the new life road of the national goods industry and the biggest crux of the lack of development of the national goods industry in the past few years. Look at the factories in the East and West. Their only backing is the bank. The interest rate on bank loans has never been as high as what is stipulated in our country. Therefore, for the same factory, their interest is less than half of ours. Since the interest is low, the cost is naturally low. In the competition between the two sides, no matter how hard our country's industry works, it will of course be a failure. I have repeatedly stated this point after returning from a visit to Japan to study industry, and have made every effort to appeal to the national goods industry. However, the government has not promulgated statutory interest rates, so it has not been implemented. I have witnessed the prevalence of high interest rates and the national goods industry's painful burden, and I am often afraid. The industrial decline has reached this point. The method of revival is of course not limited to one, but reducing interest rates has been generally recognized by all insightful people. The economic group of the Fifth National Congress has been able to grasp the key points of rescuing the industry and make fundamental plans. The reporter believes that this is indeed the only new life road for the national goods industry.

The Name of National Goods Should Be Corrected 191

— Qiu Lang

Confucius said in the Analects: "It must be the rectification of names." It can be seen that the names of things must first be specified. If things do not have a clearly defined name and are just called randomly, over time, they will inevitably be misunderstood and make the public deeply imprint bad impressions. If it is not corrected permanently, it is neither the way to rectify names nor will it be laughed at by foreign countries.

Many of the items in national goods are made in this country, but they are prefixed with the word "foreign," such as foreign fire, foreign candles, foreign umbrellas, foreign soap, etc. There are too many examples to list. These items are not imported, so I don't know why they must be prefixed with the word "foreign." It is really wronged! Moreover, it is too contradictory to the meaning of promoting national goods! In my opinion, the names of these items all need to be corrected as soon as possible. For example, "foreign fire" can be changed to "matches," "foreign umbrellas" can be changed to "sun umbrellas," "foreign soap" can be changed to "soap," and "foreign candles" can be changed to "candles" (if this name is considered inappropriate, it can be changed again). Then, a fixed term for domestic products will be specified, and it will be much better to call it out, and the suspicion of domestic products being falsely labeled with the name "foreign" will be avoided.

It is very undesirable. When our national goods factories start, they should absolutely avoid it to avoid being criticized by knowledgeable people.

A Visit to the Shanghai Cement Factory 194

— Li Guanghuang

Having previously visited the Shanghai Cement Factory owned by Chinese merchants, I wrote a brief account. Recently, seeing the world situation becoming increasingly urgent, cement, being the foundation of construction and as important as coal and iron as an essential element of modern industry, its production and sales have a tremendous impact on the prosperity and decline of a nation's industry. Therefore, I specially record this for the consideration of my countrymen.

The company's factory is located in the suburbs near Longhua Town in western Shanghai. If you wish to visit, first go to the Shanghai Cement Company at 6 Sichuan Road, Shanghai, to make arrangements with the office. They will designate a date and send someone to provide a tour.

The factory site is located south of the China National Aviation Corporation's airfield. A cinder road has been built to connect to Longhua Town, allowing vehicles to reach the gate directly. The surrounding area is filled with employee residences, forming a distinct town. Upon entering, one must fill out the visitor's book and wait briefly in the reception room. Soon, someone will appear to lead the tour of the various sections. Now, I will describe the cement manufacturing process step by step, which may make it clearer.

Cement is also known as 洋灰 (yáng huī), and in English, it's called Cement. It is also translated as 水門汀 (shuǐ mén tīng) or 士敏土 (shì mǐn tǔ). The main raw materials are limestone and clay, which are abundant in the Yangtze River basin of China. The factory unloads these two raw materials from the riverbank and separately loads them into small carts. The carts are marked with white characters to indicate their contents, and the number of carts is proportional to the quantity of each material. Simultaneously, the carts are driven by machinery along the rails directly into the factory. The carts are made of iron, shaped like buckets, and called transport buckets. Once inside the building, the raw materials are automatically dumped into steel ball mills. The empty buckets then return to the riverbank in a continuous cycle. The stone and clay are mixed and ground finely in the mills and then dropped into continuous kilns for burning. The kilns are shaped like cylinders, quite long, and there are two of them, lying parallel horizontally on the ground. They operate alternately, switching once a day. One end has a tall chimney that rises outside the building, and the other end has an opening to observe the fire, as the burning requires a specific temperature. I found it particularly dazzling to look at, so the guide took a colored glass frame from the side for me to look through, and indeed, it did not hurt the eyes and allowed me to know the temperature of the burning from the different flames. When the kiln fire is sufficient, it must be removed to cool, then ground into powder, and after screening, it becomes cement. It is packed into barrels for shipment. The trademark is an elephant. The daily output is about 1,500 barrels. Because the factory is located on the bank of the Huangpu River, it has its own wharf, making transportation convenient. However, due to the competition from foreign goods on the market, I heard that the sales of this product are greatly affected.

As for the power source for all the machinery in the factory, it comes from a steam turbine, with a voltage of 220V, a current of 4000A per line, and a power of 1500 K.A.V., which is equivalent to about 866 K.W (kilowatts, abbreviated as kW). This is sufficient for the entire factory's operation.

I must also make it clear that photography is prohibited inside the factory. The tour takes about two hours. Seeing this emerging industry in China makes me feel very gratified.

Please Printing Industry Do Your Best to Use National Paper 195

— Yihong

Here are the names of paper mills established by Chinese people and the types of products they produce, based on what I know:

Factory Name 196

— Product Types

Longzhang: Longzhang Lian Shi Paper, Daolin Paper (This is a new product with excellent quality)

Tianzhang: Daolin Paper, Drawing Paper, Cover Paper (Although the Tianzhang Paper Mill is temporarily suspended, there is still a lot of stock on the market)

Jiangnan: Lian Shi Paper, Mao Bian Paper (There is also a type of Lian Shi Paper that is very sturdy and can be written on with ink pens)

Dazhonghua: Same as above

Senji: Same as above

According to the various types of paper listed in the table above (although newsprint is still being manufactured in China and has not yet been released), they are already very suitable for various printed materials and can replace foreign paper. The price is also cheaper than foreign paper.

It is truly heartbreaking that I know some people in the printing industry and paper users are still indifferent, not paying attention, and not advocating for the use of national paper. Look—general printed materials on the market can very well be printed with national paper, yet they are always using foreign paper. Foreign paper probably accounts for 70-80% of the total.

I know that the following situations may be some of the reasons why printing houses and paper users are not making every effort to use national paper:

1. Relationship between printing houses and paper stores: Printing houses have established relationships with paper stores for the exchange of goods, so it is very convenient for printing houses to obtain paper from these stores. However, some paper stores do not have the specific type of national paper needed, so they can only supply foreign paper. Printing houses are too lazy to find and purchase national paper from other sources. Some printing houses obtain goods from established paper stores, or they do not need to pay in cash; if they were to obtain goods from other sources, they would have to prepare cash. Under these circumstances, printing houses seek ease and convenience and do not use national paper.

2. Paper stores stocking goods: Most paper stores deal in foreign paper, and some have established relationships with foreign companies. The constraints are similar to those mentioned in the previous point. It is somewhat troublesome to stock national paper separately. Therefore, they prefer to promote foreign paper. Perhaps the trade benefits that national paper mills provide to paper stores are not as good as those for foreign paper, so paper stores are not very willing to promote national paper. These two situations are also reasons why national paper cannot sell well.

3. Bad past impressions: In the past, the quality of national paper had not reached the highest level. Printing houses that had used it and were dissatisfied retained a contemptuous view of national paper. Regardless of how much better the current products are compared to the past, they still keep saying how bad national paper is and are unwilling to try and use it again.

4. Cold attitude: It cannot be said that there are not some people with a cold attitude, and even doing perverse things. They believe that they only need to make money themselves. What is the difference between national and foreign paper? What great difference does using national paper make to them? It is absolutely unnecessary for them to use national paper to replace foreign paper. If someone earnestly asks them to try using national paper, they will secretly laugh at them for being "silly." Or they will deliberately say: the price of national paper is too expensive; the quality is too bad; Chinese people cannot make good things, after all, foreign paper is better, and so on. The national paper samples they provide may be old, inferior, and not the latest and better products, and the price is arbitrarily increased. This kind of counter-propaganda, of course, easily diminishes people's enthusiasm for using national paper.

The above are some of the actual situations, based on what I have observed in a limited area. Now, the latest products of national paper have indeed improved a lot compared to the past! They can very well replace foreign paper! Please printing industry and paper users, especially government agencies, banks, companies, etc., when adding printed materials, no matter the size, pay more attention and do your best to use national paper. If you want to know the detailed information of national paper, you can directly go to the offices of the respective paper mills, or various national goods organizations, to inquire about everything and obtain the latest paper samples.

Publishing Industry

The Development Foundation of Small Newspapers 197

— Jianping

In the process of large newspapers becoming smaller and newspapers and magazines becoming more entertaining, small newspapers suddenly appeared before our readers with a lively posture. The reformed "Times Daily" and the recently published "Li Bao" can be said to be the leaders of this type of small daily newspaper in Shanghai.

Small newspapers are neither the old-fashioned tabloids of the past nor the generally tabloid-ized large newspapers. It is a light, neat, and new posture bear, standing independently among these two—or many kinds of newspapers. In the past, most old-fashioned tabloids focused on piecing together certain anecdotes, strange stories, anecdotes of great men, and romantic affairs of men and women. Its purpose was to provide the general leisure class and bored people with material for after-dinner entertainment. Although one or two newspapers in the past (such as Shanghai Bao, etc.) shifted their vision to analyze current affairs and secrets, the subject matter of anecdotes, anecdotes, and romantic events remained the main characteristic of old-fashioned tabloids.

Although the tabloid-ized large newspapers are not entirely focused on narrating anecdotes of important people and romantic affairs of famous prostitutes like the old-fashioned tabloids, the subjects and focus of their descriptions are still mainly on sports news, male and female events, and other interesting content. Although the purpose of the above two types of newspapers is the same, to attract the general leisure class and certain shop clerks and small businessmen, in our view, they cannot be regarded as small newspapers.

In our view, a so-called small newspaper should at least have the following conditions:

1. Accurate and clear, without the cumbersome nature of large newspapers, but with the richness of large newspapers;

2. Simple and economical, so that most people can read it, understand it, and afford it;

3. Able to speak from the standpoint of the interests of the majority, and able to publish a large number of opinions and articles from workers, small shop clerks, and middle school students;

4. Able to educate the public and lead the public with a solemn attitude.

Therefore, under these conditions, it must have concise and incisive editorials, essential and systematic political news, international news, and social news every day. It is best to summarize and condense the generally important political news and international news in an orderly and systematic manner every day, and analyze and dissect it in the most concise style. Occasionally insert current affairs cartoons so that readers can grasp the center of transformation in extremely complex international events, saving themselves from having to understand or explore in a wide range of news. Secondly, it must write articles in an extremely light style. It is best to use simplified characters and frequently publish the works of middle school students, shop clerks, and workers, or describe interesting events related to their daily lives: such as works like "Ye Zhongfang's Confession." At the same time, it is necessary to set up "Youth Mailbox" or "Worker Mailbox" so that the general public has a place to speak, and can solve difficult problems for these majority of readers at any time according to their environment. The last point is that it should publish more reliable political news, social news, and cultural news within a certain possible range, and always remember to fight for the interests of the majority. Therefore, the conditions for the establishment of small newspapers are not only in its simplicity and lightness; but in its ability to approach the public and grasp the public. Because simple and cheap are indeed one of the factors that make a small newspaper a small newspaper; but gaining the support of the public and taking on the task of educating and leading the public is the only foundation for the establishment and development of small newspapers. Without this foundation, small newspapers, even if they are extremely small, cannot exist and develop.

Therefore, in the current Chinese news industry, which is using newer methods to approach the vast readership, I believe that if progressive intellectuals can adhere to their claims of approaching the public and educating the public under the oppression of various economic, political, and personnel conditions; constantly maintain their certain attitude and improve the content of their newspapers; then the development foundation of small newspapers will inevitably be consolidated day by day.

The German Book Trade Exchange 198

— Tang Keming

Due to the economic depression, the publishing industry, like other enterprises, has fallen into extreme panic. Publishers do not want to organize the publishing methods in a sound manner, but only engage in cutthroat competition in business, and the result will naturally be downhill, without any improvement. Here, I would like to introduce to readers and publishers the world's most perfect book distribution organization—the German exchange system.

A hundred years ago, the world's most perfect book distribution organization already existed in Leipzig, Germany—that is, the exchange system. The foundation of this was first laid by Germany's three major booksellers: Horvath of Potstan, Campe of Nuremberg, and Voight of Fmenau. The initial address was in Richter's coffee shop, and later moved to the classroom of the seminary. At that time, all booksellers who came to Huabi City used this place as a market. The initiators provided the necessary equipment and items, and then the organization of the exchange began. Until 1836, the organization formally had a fixed building.

Members under the jurisdiction of the organization must abide by the regulations and recognize the traditional habits of the book industry. The book trade exchange, in German, is called Borsenverein. The regulations originally formulated aimed to benefit the book industry to the greatest extent. Not only was it so on the surface, but in fact, the organization had indeed become the most active machine for developing the book industry.

They have a central office for discussing many important business issues. During this period, the most difficult thing for publishers and booksellers was the lack of copyright protection for books. It is interesting and noteworthy that Leipzig's becoming the center of the book industry fifty years ago was partly due to the strict restrictions on private printing of books. As early as 1773, the issuance and sale of privately printed books was officially prohibited in the Leipzig book market. Therefore, publishing a new book in Leipzig was more trustworthy than going to Frankfurt (Leipzig's commercial rival). In addition, the unanimous ban of North German booksellers from entering the Frankfurt market a few years ago made the book industry in Leipzig flourish. Even today, the number of new books published in Berlin is greater than in Leipzig, but Leipzig has always remained the publishing center of the German book industry.

When the book trade exchange began, there were only 108 members, but their efforts increased with each passing year, and today the number of members exceeds 500.

Various advances and improvements have prompted publishers from other parts of Germany to bring funds to Leipzig to seek new life, and the book trade exchange has become increasingly prosperous.

The need for agents came with the development of the market business. At first, only the publishers felt it, and gradually the booksellers also had this need. Now, members of the book trade exchange who do not live in Leipzig, whether publishers or booksellers, all hire an agent. This system has not only made Leipzig the center of book production, but also the center of book distribution!

In the course of gradual progress, the book trade exchange immediately felt the need to issue a commercial newspaper. In 1835, a newspaper called "German Bookselling Industry Exchange Price List" appeared. In 1867, it was changed to a daily publication. The content includes new book advertisements, book descriptions, bookstore reports, trial reading coupons, etc. In this way, there is a close connection between the exchange, publishers, and booksellers every day. Especially for booksellers, they can purchase books step by step without being at a loss, so efficiency and order have been greatly improved.

As a result, there is now a formal gazette that provides a summary description of more than 1,300 organizations related to the German book industry. When a bookstore is discovered, it outlines the type of business, the names of the shareholders, and the agents it employs in a bird's-eye view.

In short, the book trade exchange is a very complex institution, but it represents great success in book distribution methods. The United States imitated it, and there is an organization similar to the Borsenverein in New York, called the Bookseller's Clearing House. Other countries such as England, France, and the Netherlands also tend to follow suit.

For the sake of clarity, let us assume the procedure for purchasing books to clarify the book trade exchange system.

For example, there is a bookseller in Hamburg who wants to buy books published in Mönchengladbach and Frankfurt. Every bookseller has a form. The format of this form is generally uniform, and the size is no more than three inches long and four inches wide. Now, the original style of this form is copied as follows: (see the form arranged below)

There are ordinary and expedited forms. The latter has a "ten" mark, which needs to be processed urgently. Generally, after receiving it, it will be mailed back on the same day.

Now, if you want to buy a certain book, fill in the name of the publisher in the corner of the form, and fill in the title of the book you want to buy in the blank space. After filling out several forms, the bookseller in Hamburg mails them not to Mönchengladbach and Frankfurt, where the books are published, but to Leipzig. Write the name of the publisher's agent in Leipzig on the envelope. After the agent receives this form, he goes to the office to pack the books the other party needs into a parcel and hands it over to the agent of the Hamburg bookseller in Leipzig. Then take it to the Packet Auctansch Stelle to mail it back to its owner. In theory, after the parcel is paid, the payment for the book must be paid, but there is usually a delay of about a week. Therefore, both parties need a way to keep accounts, just like banks.

After the expedited form is completed, then pay attention to the ordinary form. The process is the same as the above method, and the procedure is only completed after the parcel arrives in the hands of the bookseller's agent, and the book is mailed to its client.

Note (the content in parentheses is English notes)

Using the exchange system to purchase books has the following three advantages:

(1) All booksellers' forms are sent in one envelope to one place (Leipzig).

(2) Booksellers can save the trouble of sending drafts to many publishers, while publishers can avoid recording the procedures for receiving drafts from more than a hundred bookstores or booksellers.

(3) Sending in bulk can also save a lot of postage.

Bookstore Miscellany (Continued) 199

— Li Hengzhi

Secondly, most new bookstores are facing financial difficulties, forcing them to live within their means. This contradicts the editor-in-chief's publishing plans, often resulting in the editor-in-chief approving manuscripts or even issuing payment slips, while the accounting department under the general manager insists on withholding payment. In the past, incidents of general managers fighting with authors or editors due to this were common. However, there are also many cases where the general manager and publishing are integrated. In those bookstores where the boss also serves as the general manager, naturally there are no problems.

To be frank, the new book industry is still in its pioneering stage, especially now, during this turbulent time. The general manager's responsibility is immense, and the rise and fall of many bookstores depend on the general manager. The general manager often concurrently serves as the sales director, and some even don't have a sales director, leaving all sales matters to be handled solely by the general manager. This has a significant impact on the bookstore's business. Even with good books, without good promotion, books cannot become widely known on their own. Unfortunately, there are still cases of general managers becoming bureaucratic and corrupt in new bookstores. Some general managers engage in "petty trading," such as printing extra copies of easily sold books for their own personal gain, or establishing their own paper mills or printing houses and transacting with the bookstores they manage, ensuring that their bookstores never suffer any losses. Some bookstore general managers embezzle public funds, while others become corrupt, as if becoming a bookstore general manager is like climbing the ladder to officialdom, spending their days mingling in official circles. Some even think they are already great tycoons, so they spend their days booking rooms to play mahjong and summoning servants. Although this may seem like personal matters, how much loss does it cause to the publishing and cultural industries?

(5) Store Employees

The organizational structure of new bookstores varies in size, so the situation of store employees also differs greatly. Larger bookstores have a more complex division of labor, and there are more types of employees. For example, in large bookstores such as Commercial Press and Zhonghua Book Company, the division of labor is quite detailed. Even though they are all employees, the nature of their work, from department heads to junior clerks, is completely different. However, at the same time, most new bookstores, such as those lining the Fourth Road, are not large in scale. Therefore, the duties of the so-called store employees are mostly similar. In some cases, the boss, manager, and employee are all the same person (of course, there are also a few separate employees). The status of employees in these family-run bookstores is naturally different from that in large bookstores.

Generally speaking, in new bookstores that are neither too large nor too small, store employees are of considerable importance. This is because, in these bookstores, apart from the manager and a few other personnel, it is these store employees who support the entire business. Because their division of labor is not large, their nature is also similar. Moreover, today's new bookstores are mostly of this type, so we can use them as an example to discuss some of the more interesting situations.

First, let's talk about the source of store employees. Because the history of new bookstores is still short, there are not many store employees who were completely created to meet the needs of new bookstores. Many bookstore employees are still clerks from old-style bookstores. These people are called "insiders," while others are called "outsiders." This also shows the non-modern nature of the operating methods of new bookstores. However, this is only true for the majority. It is not to say that new bookstores do not have new-style employees. On the contrary, they are gradually developing, and those employees who have transitioned from old-style bookstores are likely to be eliminated.

The power to hire employees lies in the hands of the general manager or manager, so the general manager or manager plays a significant role in the decision of who to hire. Because most new bookstores have not yet embarked on the path of modern organization, "feudal" factors are still significant. This is reflected in the hiring of employees through the referral of fellow villagers and relatives. You see, even in the Kaifeng Bookstore, are not most of the employees from Shaoxing? In the Modern Bookstore during the Hong Xuefan era, were not most of the employees from Ningbo? Furthermore, in smaller new bookstores, it goes without saying that many employees are said to be related to the Li family.

Even more backward than this situation is the existence of the apprenticeship system. In many bookstores, most of the employees are apprentices, and in some cases, all of them are apprentices. This is a major misunderstanding on the part of new bookstore operators. They believe that the book industry is the same as other retail businesses and can use "cheap and easily controlled" apprentices to handle all duties. As a result, most of the store employees in new bookstores are half-baked, and some cannot even read many words. When you walk into these bookstores, not only do the employees not know how to serve you, but sometimes when you ask them if they have a certain type of book, they will bring you a completely opposite book. If you specifically ask them for a certain book, even if the book is right in front of them, they will stare blankly and not know what to do, and may even say that they don't have it. How can such people develop the new book industry? It is truly difficult.

It seems that in order to adapt to the times, various bookstores once competed to hire female store employees. In Japan, almost all of the employees in large bookstores such as Maruzen and Sanseido are female (most of the male employees are in higher-level command positions), and their abilities are mostly stronger than those of Chinese male employees. For example, if you ask them for the complete works of Tolstoy, they will go on to recommend the complete works of Dostoevsky, etc. They will definitely know where every book in their store is located. Sometimes, if they don't have the book, they will even tell you where you can buy it. However, in China, female employees are generally still referred to as mere decorations, even in bookstores, which are cultural enterprises. The first bookstore to hire female store employees was the Beauty Bookstore founded by Dr. Zhang Jingsheng. The female store employees there seemed to only know Dr. Zhang's few major works, making bookworms feel like country bumpkins entering a dance hall when they entered the Beauty Bookstore. Later, the trend of hiring female employees in various industries in Shanghai became more open, and people were less curious about female store employees in bookstores. However, according to my personal opinion, it seems that the abilities of female store employees in general are still not very good, and they still seem to be somewhat of a decoration. When the Daitong Bookstore completed the construction of its new sales department, there were many female employees in various departments. These female employees seemed somewhat reluctant to interact with customers. As the prosperity of the Daitong Bookstore faded, the female employees, like vases, soon disappeared. When the Modern Bookstore expanded its sales department, it also had a group of "beautiful" female employees. Some poor friends who wanted to go inside to browse through literary books ended up backing away. Sometimes, when customers made purchases from them, several female employees showed a kind of shyness. Like the Daitong Bookstore, the female employees of the Modern Bookstore soon disappeared as well. This further shows that female store employees seem to be a kind of decoration for bookstores when they are wealthy. Nowadays, not many bookstores hire female store employees, and the abilities of female store employees have not increased either. (To be continued)

After publication, a fee of three to four yuan will be paid per thousand words. Regardless of whether or not a submission is published, it will not be returned unless it is accompanied by sufficient postage.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Trivial Words

Politicians' Promises 200

— Xing An

The British general election for the Lower House was held on the 14th. In the preceding days, the campaign was very intense. Judging by the situation, this election is particularly unfavorable to the government. The Labor Party's power is quite strong in various industrial areas. Cabinet ministers who are candidates in industrial areas are in a very awkward position. In particular, Privy Councilor MacDonald, the leader of the National Labor Party, is unable to gain people's trust. When MacDonald recently delivered a campaign speech in the West Ham port miners' area, disturbances frequently occurred at the venue, causing him to retreat before finishing his speech. There were even those who shouted at MacDonald when he left the venue. MacDonald was elected as a Member of Parliament by the miners of the West Ham district. The reason why he is not trusted this time is that none of the promises MacDonald made have been fulfilled. On international issues, military issues, and tariff issues, MacDonald went back on his word. On the wage issue and the means test issue, which are most needed by the people, MacDonald made various promises beforehand, but none of them were fulfilled afterward. Therefore, it is no wonder that the miners collectively criticized MacDonald for his current offer of various promises, and no longer trusted him.

What enables a politician (and political parties) to gain people's trust is not how pleasant their promises sound before taking office, but their ability to fulfill their promises after taking office. No matter how many sweet words a politician says to the people during the election campaign, if they go back on their word after gaining the support of the people, they will immediately lose the trust of the people. MacDonald is the best example. MacDonald was deeply supported by the West Ham miners in the previous election, but this time he was criticized because he failed to fulfill his previous promises. Xingwei, the candidate running against MacDonald in the West Ham district, said that he reaps what he sows, which is quite correct. Although the people may be fooled for a while, how can they be deceived afterward? Once you take office, your true colors will be revealed. Not only will you forget your previous oaths, but you will also leave the promises you made to the people behind. As a result, you will lose all public support. The people will scold you and complain about you. Some who cannot bear it will overthrow you. It can be seen that a politician's promises should not be made lightly unless they are made in good faith. Under the watchful eyes of all, you cannot escape the people's supervision.

Untitled 201

— Jiang Dejing

Those undulating memories, like a small brown worm, as soon as there is a moment of tranquility in my heart, slowly crawl up, crawling to the depths of my heart.

The fleeting years, carrying those vague past events, seem to be in a fog, gradually drifting away, drifting away, leaving only some vague shadows. I want these shadows to report how the fleeting years are so heartbreaking, I want to get rid of them, but that little brown worm brings them slowly crawling up to my heart again.

That little worm uses her delicate claws to hook the strings of my heart, playing very subtle music. I bow my head and use all my strength to understand its rhythm - so low, telling its aspirations and fantasies, hopes and nostalgia. The joy of the past is just the setting sun on the top of the mountain, covering the whole world with beautiful colors for a moment. But it easily sinks into the night, that terrible night; all are cold-eyed stars, twinkling, laughing at each other.

I wander, listening to such a mournful music, but I can no longer listen to it, it will make me shed tears. I want to stand on the high ridge of Wanren, howl at the boundless sky, cut through the jade-like long sky, and fly to the world after the sky. There, there are no fleeting years; the little brown worm will never crawl up to my heart.

Goddess 202

— Jiang Mi

The five goddesses, since they refined the five-colored stones, repaired the missing part of the sky, created the sun, and drove away the "darkness", they played silent music in this beautiful world. I don’t know how many years have passed, and they are hard to remember. Just look at the moon, which is round and missing, and then missing and round again. (II)

Guest 203

— Si Quan

This has always been a warm pavilion, on the side of the flower hall. Thick velvet curtains covered the window, and there was no light in the side alley behind it, so the warm pavilion was extremely dark. In summer, this room is locked up. In winter, the master and madam spread a smoking set on the mandarin duck couch, and the two of them stayed in seclusion inside all day long. The master was a tall, thin man, holding only a water pipe at this time, wandering in front of the couch. The area of the warm pavilion was not two fathoms wide, and the mandarin duck couch almost occupied one-third of the space. With the addition of the tea table and backrests, there were only a few square feet of space left in front of the couch. Therefore, the master could not swagger and pace around like he did in the flower hall. He almost walked three steps with his heels touching his toes, and then had to turn around. However, his attention was now completely focused on his daughter. A paper match was about to burn his fingertips, but he had not taken a puff of smoke, and he had walked back and forth so naturally. The madam, on the other hand, was a tall, fat, middle-aged woman whose weight increased every day. She lay on the upper part of the mandarin duck couch, smoking, looking like a pile of cotton batting, or a large piece of luggage brought back from a long journey. The madam was tall and fat even before she got married, and now she dared not easily say the word "fat". She found it quite difficult to turn around to smoke, so usually the master would do the work at the lower end of the couch, and the madam only had to bring the mouthpiece to her lips and close her eyes to take a refreshing puff. Today, after arguing with the master, she was unwilling to admit defeat. Since the master refused to help, she had no choice but to do it herself. But before she could finish smoking a pipe, the pile of cotton batting was already like an engine in rapid progress.

The paper match in the master's hand burned his finger, and he suddenly woke up, stopped wandering, and rushed to his wife's ear, questioning, "What are we going to do about this matter?"

The madam had not had enough pleasure, and could not support her body, which weighed more than twice that of the master, on its side. She used all her strength to push the smoking set away, and rolled her body to face the ceiling, finally breathing a sigh of relief:

"The daughter is not raised by me alone, what a joke!" After saying that, she felt that her tone was too soft, and suddenly sat up from the mandarin duck couch. Because the master was unprepared, she almost bumped into him head-on. She then said to the master's face: "Ask you, the father! If you don't raise and teach her, it's the father's fault. You still have the face to ask me, how can you ask that! You old..." She couldn't find a suitable name for a moment, because crude and vulgar curses would ultimately cause her to lose her "madam" status, so she stopped and lay back down, breathing two comfortable breaths.

"If you don't raise and teach her, it's the father's fault?" The master interjected; "I've read so many books, but I'm not as good as you. If you don't raise and teach her, it's the father's fault? With you, this mother, standing in front of me, is there still a father? Now that she's done this shameless thing, you're thinking of If you don't raise and teach her, it's the father's fault!"

The master took out another paper match from the smoking set, lit it with the dim green flame of the lamp, and sat down on the lower part of the mandarin duck couch to smoke the water pipe. The madam rolled over to face the master, but couldn't think of anything to retort, so she yawned, dragged the smoking set closer, and started smoking.

At this moment, the young servant who was in charge of the warm pavilion poked his head in - perhaps he had been standing outside the pavilion for a long time, listening to the couple's argument - and reported softly: "Uncle!"

The master waved his paper match: "Tell him I'm not seeing guests."

The madam, however, seized the master's mistake and said, "Not seeing guests? What kind of important official are you pretending to be! He's my brother, and I want to see him! Afu, please ask the uncle to come in." The madam wanted to turn around, but the opium suddenly flared up on the lamp.

Afu's body had just retreated, and the uncle had already stepped into the warm pavilion. He made a deep bow to his sister's husband, and the master had no choice but to put down the water pipe and return the bow, taking the opportunity to give the guest the lower seat and retreating to sit on the backrest in front of the window.

"Brother," The madam had an extra helper. Although she had not had enough pleasure, her voice naturally became rougher: "You be the judge for me: You came to propose marriage for Xiaofeng, but he wouldn't agree no matter what. In fact, such a family would not disgrace your official position; now that Xiaofeng has escaped, uh, left, it's my fault again. Brother, you be the judge for me!" The madam, still angry, pointed her finger at the master from a distance.

The uncle first gave a burst of laughter: "I came after hearing the news. Now is not the time to delay. We should find Xiaofeng back first. Brother-in-law, what do you think?" He thought for a moment: "Although this is not something unclean, it is still your face, brother-in-law, if the news spreads." The uncle said, word by word, with a chuckle, waiting for his brother-in-law's reply.

The brother-in-law raised his head, without interjecting. The madam, however, said: "What's the use of saying more? The daughter is not raised by me alone, let her go!"

"Sister, don't add fuel to the fire!" The uncle put on a serious face, "This is a man's business, and brother-in-law will always think of a solution slowly; however, now is not the time to delay..." He stood up from the mandarin duck couch and slowly walked to the window.

The brother-in-law seemed embarrassed to continue being cold, "Do as you see fit! I'll pretend I didn't raise this daughter!" Saying that, he left the warm pavilion on his own.

The uncle followed him to the entrance of the warm pavilion, saw his brother-in-law's shadow enter the flower hall, turned around and stuck his tongue out at his sister: "Then it's easy to handle, leave it to me, your uncle." He patted his chest with his right hand.

"This old ghost never agrees with me!" The madam smiled victoriously, wriggling her bloated body and saying to the uncle, "Brother, lie down for a while!"

A Visit to Xuanwu Lake 204

— Yang Zhongshuo

Leaving Xuanwu Gate, that straight road, tightly wrapped in green willows, seemed even more magnificent and full of vigor.

I have a bit of an eccentricity. I have never been very fond of being blindly fashionable. It's the same when I look at scenery. No matter whether the places that people praise and admire are historical sites or scenic spots, I seem to regard them with indifference and remain unmoved. This kind of unsociable narrow-mindedness may be due to heredity, but it is also partly due to my deeper involvement in the world. For example, when I was in Hangzhou a few years ago, I gathered a few friends to visit Liulang Wenying and Quyuan Fenghe because I was shocked by their names. Before I went, I always thought that these places must be extraordinary, but the result was a disappointing return.

But this time I visited Xuanwu, and I felt very happy. It's been almost half a year since I came to Nanjing. Apart from going to Sun Yat-sen's Mausoleum out of necessity, it can be said that I haven't left my house. Xuanwu Lake is naturally the first time I've visited it.

It is said that the beauty of Xuanwu Lake lies in the lotus flowers all over the lake. However, at this moment, not only have the lotus flowers long since withered, but even the lotus leaves have turned yellow and died.

Although the lotus flowers have withered and the lotus leaves have died, Xuanwu in the late autumn has a desolate and poignant beauty. I remember someone comparing the West Lake in spring to a plump woman, then Xuanwu in late autumn should be a petite, dignified, and rather serious girl.

It was a holiday weekend. There was a shower in the morning, and although the rain stopped in the afternoon, the sky was still gloomy and depressing. However, the number of tourists did not decrease due to the cloudy weather.

We chose a place where we could both enjoy the scenery and avoid the cold wind, and we began to talk without any purpose.

"In fact, the beauty of Xuanwu lies in the fact that it has the name of a lake but not the reality of a lake. You say it is a lake, but it does not have the conditions that a lake must have. When you step into Xuanwu Gate, all you see are a few patches of shallow water mixed in with withered lotus flowers. You simply can't find any traces of a lake. Everyone knows that the most important condition for constituting a lake is water. Those few patches of shallow water in Xuanwu Lake really can't meet the name of a lake, but its beauty lies in this point. If Xuanwu was a reservoir lake with green water, then the graceful beauty would not exist."

The above is a discussion by Lao Yu. To avoid disputes, we all remained silent, because we all knew that Lao Yu's personality was very strong.

However, in my opinion, the characteristic of Xuanwu is not in the lake itself, but in the background that constitutes its characteristics, such as the majestic and beautiful mountain scenery, the ancient and mottled city walls, and the withered branches and leaves all over the lake, which together create this intricate scenery woven by man and nature.

If you haven't visited Xuanwu Lake, you will never feel the greatness of the Nanjing city walls. That winding giant wall stands there so somber and solemnly, adding a lot of color to this famous lake!

Some people say that Xuanwu Lake is a bit like Beihai in the ancient capital. In the late summer and early autumn, the beautiful lotus flowers and the green lotus leaves all have the characteristics of Beihai. Unfortunately, at this moment, the lotus flowers are withered and decayed, so I can't compare Beihai and Xuanwu. This may not be a lack of my visit to Xuanwu Lake this time.

Xuanwu Lake has one more advantage than Beihai. That is to say, Beihai has lost too much artificiality, while Xuanwu has a lot of natural beauty.

We rested for a while in "Asia Park", and then we finished visiting "Europe", "America" and "Philippine" continents. We didn't go to "Australia", which is far away in the water, in order to save trouble and avoid trekking.

Song Introduction 205

Stored in the Heart

Good times are constantly flowing, good birds are constantly chirping, people's happiness is everywhere, no matter how you invest: don't even think about happiness in your heart, I guarantee you will be full of sorrow and resentment. Who to tell, who to open your mouth to, locked in your heart, a cavity of troubles, thousands of frowns. What to do! What to do! Stored in the heart. Spring goes but cannot stay long, spring comes but will not last long, people's environment, the universe, why bother to ask for it? Just focus on the present and don't care about the future, get by and don't think about it. Don't tell, don't open your mouth, keep it in your heart, no need to worry, no warehouse of frowns. Strive! Strive! Stored in the heart.

Storytelling with Stringed Instruments 208

Xia Hesheng's Three Smiles

Dunben (800) 7:00 PM to 8:00 PM

Opening Chapter "Jia Baoyu Visits Xiaoxiang Pavilion at Night"

The severe winter chill freezes into ice. The moonlight is hazy, the soul about to break. Gusts of north wind penetrate the bones. The black and cavernous Grand View Garden is cold and deserted. Baoyu walks along Flower Street. The night is late, and no sound is heard. He is carrying a lamp, all alone. Dark shadows flicker before him. He goes alone to Xiaoxiang Pavilion. To see if Miss Lin's illness has lessened. He gently knocks on the copper ring, tapping lightly. Will someone quickly come and open the door? Zijuan hears. She asks. Is it the Second Master Baoyu wanting to enter? She hastily opens the door. Please be careful, the cold of the deep night shows no mercy. Thank you, Sister, for your concern. I will never forget your great kindness. It is only because I am worried about your Miss Lin. That is why I have come in the quiet of the night. He has arrived by the bedside. Seeing her, gasping for breath, tears streaming down her face. One calls out "Sister Lin." The other calls out "Cousin." Her almond eyes open slightly, unable to see clearly, "Cousin, your Second Sister-in-law treats me too harshly. Her words are wild, confusing right and wrong. Although Grandmother loves me dearly. Alas, I cannot go to pay my respects." "You and I, the debts of a past life are being settled in this life. Please do not look at this ill-fated person." "Sister, put aside all your worries. Do not take things too lightly. I advise you to eat three meals a day. Add clothes to keep warm. I advise you to sleep early at night. Drink more soup and supplements. I advise you, do not listen to what your sisters say. They are, like half-true, half-jesting. I advise you, take care of your body and mind, and take care. Do not think about the old home in Yangzhou." Hearing these words. Tears stream down. The fated enemy is most attentive to me. "Cousin, please return early to Yi Hong Yuan. Tears soak the fragrant silk handkerchief." "This body may not be too adrift."

Movie

Tibet to Nanjing 212

Tibet to Nanjing, tens of thousands of miles apart, with dangerous roads and no western transport line, so the Tibetan side cannot imagine the majesty of Nanjing, and the people of Nanjing cannot understand the mysterious nature of Tibet, but now there is a shocking news, that the entire mysterious Tibet has been moved to the capital of Nanjing.

It turns out that the film "Mysterious Tibet" of the Yueming Company was taken to Nanjing by Li Faxi yesterday.

"Mysterious Tibet" can not only be said to be the biggest gain of Yueming Company in 1935, but also can be said to be the only work in the Chinese film industry. In the environment of Jia Bao and the serious national crisis, the border issue is the focus of national attention, especially Tibet, a region containing countless wonderful stories, every Chinese has a mysterious yearning, mysterious but unable to know its mystery, the degree of mystery is indescribable.

"Mysterious Tibet" not only reveals the mysterious face, but also analyzes the inner layer of mystery. This film is a must-see for every citizen.

"Mysterious Tibet" is preparing to invite the leaders of the Five Alliances to watch it at the Lizhi Society or the Capital Theater in Nanjing, so that the virtuous people of the country can first have an impression of the ancient country's border, and then immediately perform in the capital and Shanghai.

Backstage of Broadway 214

—Great Shanghai Reflection

Realistic Picture in "Boatman's House" 215

Foreign goods are transported to China in large quantities, and all Chinese industries are stagnant! Judging from cotton yarn alone, the annual imports are always more than hundreds of thousands of tons. In this way, Chinese factories can only close down, and where will a large number of workers go to eat? So all kinds of cruel labor-capital struggles are placed before our eyes, and the news of families losing their jobs and starving to death has also been seen by us. There are still many more cruel things that we cannot easily see, and there are more than we can imagine.

Gao Gufei encountered such cruel things in "Boatman's Daughter." That day, his factory suddenly stopped work. In order to eat, he had to gather all the workers for a meeting to demand that the factory resume work. At the gate of the factory, they shouted loudly: "We all have families, what should we do in the future?

"We will have no food tomorrow, we can't starve to death, can we?"

The veins on Gao Zhanfei's head were popping out, and the roaring sound made the blood vessels of the onlookers boil. Friends, this is a very realistic picture.

Yangtze River Drama Society Established 216

Liu Tan, who has been silent for a long time, seems to be active again recently. The drama societies are staging one after another, and the amateur actors' "Nora" and "The Government Inspector" have won the support of a wide audience, showing the unlimited future of the Chinese drama world. In order to love drama, in order to establish the Chinese drama world more firmly, more than 20 amateur actors including Wang Limin and He Kangli initiated a Yangtze River Drama Society. There was such a proposal a few months ago. The initiators were busy with the public performances of "Nora" and "The Government Inspector", so they were delayed. At the same time, they realized from the response of this public performance that the current drama seats were still too aristocratic. They must make it more popular and more universal within the possible scope, so that everyone can see more noble dramas at the lowest price. Now, after several meetings, the Yangtze River Drama Society has announced its establishment, and has decided to choose one of the two plays "The Tragedy of Lan Gu's Marriage" and "The Hypocrite" for the first public performance. The director has also been decided to be Shen Xiling, one of the directors of "The Government Inspector".
